See the NOTICE file distributed with\\n4:  * this work for additional information regarding copyright ownership.\\n5:  * The ASF licenses this file to You under the Apache License, Version 2.0\\n6:  * (the \\\"License\\\"); you may not use this file except in compliance with\\n7:  * the License. The schema is given below:\\n47:  *\\n48:  * RecordBatch =>\\n49:  *  BaseOffset => Int64\\n50:  *  Length => Int32\\n51:  *  PartitionLeaderEpoch => Int32\\n52:  *  Magic => Int8\\n53:  *  CRC => Uint32\\n54:  *  Attributes => Int16\\n55:  *  LastOffsetDelta => Int32 // also serves as LastSequenceDelta\\n56:  *  BaseTimestamp => Int64\\n57:  *  MaxTimestamp => Int64\\n58:  *  ProducerId => Int64\\n59:  *  ProducerEpoch => Int16\\n60:  *  BaseSequence => Int32\\n61:  *  RecordsCount => Int32\\n62:  *  Records => [Record]\\n63:  *\\n64:  * Note that when compression is enabled (see attributes below), the compressed record data is serialized\\n65:  * directly following the count of the number of records.\\n66:  *\\n67:  * The CRC covers the data from the attributes to the end of the batch (i.e. all the bytes that follow the CRC). It is\\n68:  * located after the magic byte, which means that clients must parse the magic byte before deciding how to interpret\\n69:  * the bytes between the batch length and the magic byte. The partition leader epoch field is not included in the CRC\\n70:  * computation to avoid the need to recompute the CRC when this field is assigned for every batch that is received by\\n71:  * the broker. The CRC-32C (Castagnoli) polynomial is used for the computation.\\n72:  *\\n73:  * On Compaction: Unlike the older message formats, magic v2 and above preserves the first and last offset/sequence\\n74:  * numbers from the original batch when the log is cleaned. This is required in order to be able to restore the\\n75:  * producer's state when the log is reloaded. If we did not retain the last sequence number, then following\\n76:  * a partition leader failure, once the new leader has rebuilt the producer state from the log, the next sequence\\n77:  * expected number would no longer be in sync with what was written by the client. This would cause an\\n78:  * unexpected OutOfOrderSequence error, which is typically fatal. The base sequence number must be preserved for\\n79:  * duplicate checking: the broker checks incoming Produce requests for duplicates by verifying that the first and\\n80:  * last sequence numbers of the incoming batch match the last from that producer.\\n81:  *\\n82:  * Note that if all of the records in a batch are removed during compaction, the broker may still retain an empty\\n83:  * batch header in order to preserve the producer sequence information as described above. These empty batches\\n84:  * are retained only until either a new sequence number is written by the corresponding producer or the producerId\\n85:  * is expired from lack of activity.\\n86:  *\\n87:  * There is no similar need to preserve the timestamp from the original batch after compaction. The BaseTimestamp\\n88:  * field therefore reflects the timestamp of the first record in the batch in most cases. If the batch is empty, the\\n89:  * BaseTimestamp will be set to -1 (NO_TIMESTAMP). If the delete horizon flag is set to 1, the BaseTimestamp\\n90:  * will be set to the time at which tombstone records and aborted transaction markers in the batch should be removed.\\n91:  *\\n92:  * Similarly, the MaxTimestamp field reflects the maximum timestamp of the current records if the timestamp type\\n93:  * is CREATE_TIME. For LOG_APPEND_TIME, on the other hand, the MaxTimestamp field reflects the timestamp set\\n94:  * by the broker and is preserved after compaction. Additionally, the MaxTimestamp of an empty batch always retains\\n95:  * the previous value prior to becoming empty.\\n96:  *\\n97:  * The current attributes are given below:\\n98:  *\\n99:  *  ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\\n100:  *  | Unused (7-15) | Delete Horizon Flag (6) | Control (5) | Transactional (4) | Timestamp Type (3) | Compression Type (0-2) |\\n101:  *  ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\\n102:  */\\n103: public class DefaultRecordBatch extends The schema is given below:\\n47:  *\\n48:  * RecordBatch =>\\n49:  *  BaseOffset => Int64\\n50:  *  Length => Int32\\n51:  *  PartitionLeaderEpoch => Int32\\n52:  *  Magic => Int8\\n53:  *  CRC => Uint32\\n54:  *  Attributes => Int16\\n55:  *  LastOffsetDelta => Int32 // also serves as LastSequenceDelta\\n56:  *  BaseTimestamp => Int64\\n57:  *  MaxTimestamp => Int64\\n58:  *  ProducerId => Int64\\n59:  *  ProducerEpoch => Int16\\n60:  *  BaseSequence => Int32\\n61:  *  RecordsCount => Int32\\n62:  *  Records => [Record]\\n63:  *\\n64:  * Note that when compression is enabled (see attributes below), the compressed record data is serialized\\n65:  * directly following the count of the number of records.\\n66:  *\\n67:  * The CRC covers the data from the attributes to the end of the batch (i.e. all the bytes that follow the CRC). It is\\n68:  * located after the magic byte, which means that clients must parse the magic byte before deciding how to interpret\\n69:  * the bytes between the batch length and the magic byte. The partition leader epoch field is not included in the CRC\\n70:  * computation to avoid the need to recompute the CRC when this field is assigned for every batch that is received by\\n71:  * the broker. The CRC-32C (Castagnoli) polynomial is used for the computation.\\n72:  *\\n73:  * On Compaction: Unlike the older message formats, magic v2 and above preserves the first and last offset/sequence\\n74:  * numbers from the original batch when the log is cleaned. This is required in order to be able to restore the\\n75:  * producer's state when the log is reloaded. If we did not retain the last sequence number, then following\\n76:  * a partition leader failure, once the new leader has rebuilt the producer state from the log, the next sequence\\n77:  * expected number would no longer be in sync with what was written by the client. This would cause an\\n78:  * unexpected OutOfOrderSequence error, which is typically fatal. The base sequence number must be preserved for\\n79:  * duplicate checking: the broker checks incoming Produce requests for duplicates by verifying that the first and\\n80:  * last sequence numbers of the incoming batch match the last from that producer.\\n81:  *\\n82:  * Note that if all of the records in a batch are removed during compaction, the broker may still retain an empty\\n83:  * batch header in order to preserve the producer sequence information as described above. These empty batches\\n84:  * are retained only until either a new sequence number is written by the corresponding producer or the producerId\\n85:  * is expired from lack of activity.\\n86:  *\\n87:  * There is no similar need to preserve the timestamp from the original batch after compaction. The BaseTimestamp\\n88:  * field therefore reflects the timestamp of the first record in the batch in most cases. If the batch is empty, the\\n89:  * BaseTimestamp will be set to -1 (NO_TIMESTAMP). If the delete horizon flag is set to 1, the BaseTimestamp\\n90:  * will be set to the time at which tombstone records and aborted transaction markers in the batch should be removed.\\n91:  *\\n92:  * Similarly, the MaxTimestamp field reflects the maximum timestamp of the current records if the timestamp type\\n93:  * is CREATE_TIME. For LOG_APPEND_TIME, on the other hand, the MaxTimestamp field reflects the timestamp set\\n94:  * by the broker and is preserved after compaction. Additionally, the MaxTimestamp of an empty batch always retains\\n95:  * the previous value prior to becoming empty.\\n96:  *\\n97:  * The current attributes are given below:\\n98:  *\\n99:  *  ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\\n100:  *  | Unused (7-15) | Delete Horizon Flag (6) | Control (5) | Transactional (4) | Timestamp Type (3) | Compression Type (0-2) |\\n101:  *  ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\\n102:  */\\n103: public class DefaultRecordBatch extends The schema is given below:\n47:  *\n48:  * RecordBatch =>\n49:  *  BaseOffset => Int64\n50:  *  Length => Int32\n51:  *  PartitionLeaderEpoch => Int32\n52:  *  Magic => Int8\n53:  *  CRC => Uint32\n54:  *  Attributes => Int16\n55:  *  LastOffsetDelta => Int32 // also serves as LastSequenceDelta\n56:  *  BaseTimestamp => Int64\n57:  *  MaxTimestamp => Int64\n58:  *  ProducerId => Int64\n59:  *  ProducerEpoch => Int16\n60:  *  BaseSequence => Int32\n61:  *  RecordsCount => Int32\n62:  *  Records => [Record]\n63:  *\n64:  * Note that when compression is enabled (see attributes below), the compressed record data is serialized\n65:  * directly following the count of the number of records.\n66:  *\n67:  * The CRC covers the data from the attributes to the end of the batch (i.e. all the bytes that follow the CRC). It is\n68:  * located after the magic byte, which means that clients must parse the magic byte before deciding how to interpret\n69:  * the bytes between the batch length and the magic byte. The partition leader epoch field is not included in the CRC\n70:  * computation to avoid the need to recompute the CRC when this field is assigned for every batch that is received by\n71:  * the broker. The CRC-32C (Castagnoli) polynomial is used for the computation.\n72:  *\n73:  * On Compaction: Unlike the older message formats, magic v2 and above preserves the first and last offset/sequence\n74:  * numbers from the original batch when the log is cleaned. This is required in order to be able to restore the\n75:  * producer's state when the log is reloaded. If we did not retain the last sequence number, then following\n76:  * a partition leader failure, once the new leader has rebuilt the producer state from the log, the next sequence\n77:  * expected number would no longer be in sync with what was written by the client. This would cause an\n78:  * unexpected OutOfOrderSequence error, which is typically fatal. The base sequence number must be preserved for\n79:  * duplicate checking: the broker checks incoming Produce requests for duplicates by verifying that the first and\n80:  * last sequence numbers of the incoming batch match the last from that producer.\n81:  *\n82:  * Note that if all of the records in a batch are removed during compaction, the broker may still retain an empty\n83:  * batch header in order to preserve the producer sequence information as described above. These empty batches\n84:  * are retained only until either a new sequence number is written by the corresponding producer or the producerId\n85:  * is expired from lack of activity.\n86:  *\n87:  * There is no similar need to preserve the timestamp from the original batch after compaction. The BaseTimestamp\n88:  * field therefore reflects the timestamp of the first record in the batch in most cases. If the batch is empty, the\n89:  * BaseTimestamp will be set to -1 (NO_TIMESTAMP). If the delete horizon flag is set to 1, the BaseTimestamp\n90:  * will be set to the time at which tombstone records and aborted transaction markers in the batch should be removed.\n91:  *\n92:  * Similarly, the MaxTimestamp field reflects the maximum timestamp of the current records if the timestamp type\n93:  * is CREATE_TIME. For LOG_APPEND_TIME, on the other hand, the MaxTimestamp field reflects the timestamp set\n94:  * by the broker and is preserved after compaction. Additionally, the MaxTimestamp of an empty batch always retains\n95:  * the previous value prior to becoming empty.\n96:  *\n97:  * The current attributes are given below:\n98:  *\n99:  *  ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n100:  *  | Unused (7-15) | Delete Horizon Flag (6) | Control (5) | Transactional (4) | Timestamp Type (3) | Compression Type (0-2) |\n101:  *  ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------\n102:  */\n103: public class DefaultRecordBatch extends AbstractRecordBatch In old versions of the record format (versions 0 and 1),\n * a batch consisted always of a single record if no compression was enabled, but could contain\n * many records otherwise. Newer versions (magic versions 2 and above) will generally contain many records\n * regardless of compression.\n *\n * <p>\n * <strong>Thread Safety:</strong> Implementations of this interface may not be thread-safe. Callers must\n * ensure external synchronization if the batch is accessed from multiple threads.\n * </p>\n *\n * @see DefaultRecordBatch for the magic v2 implementation\n * @see MemoryRecords for in-memory collections of record batches\n */\npublic interface RecordBatch extends Iterable<Record> {\n\n    /**\n     * The \"magic\" values\n     */\n    byte MAGIC_VALUE_V0 = 0;\n    byte MAGIC_VALUE_V1 = 1;\n    byte MAGIC_VALUE_V2 = 2;\n\n    /**\n     * The current \"magic\" value\n     */\n    byte CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE = MAGIC_VALUE_V2;\n\n    /**\n     * Timestamp value for records without a timestamp\n     */\n    long NO_TIMESTAMP = -1L;\n\n    /**\n     * Values used in the v2 record format by non-idempotent/non-transactional producers or when\n     * up-converting from an older format.\n     */\n    long NO_PRODUCER_ID = -1L;\n    short NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH = -1;\n    int NO_SEQUENCE = -1;\n\n    /**\n     * Used to indicate an unknown leader epoch, which will be the case when the record set is\n     * first created by the producer.\n     */\n    int NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH = -1;\n\n    /**\n     * Check whether the checksum of this batch is correct.\n     *\n     * @return true if the checksum is valid, false otherwise\n     */\n    boolean isValid();\n\n    /**\n     * Raise an exception if the checksum is not valid.\n     *\n     * @throws org.apache.kafka.common.errors.CorruptRecordException if the checksum validation fails\n     */\n    void ensureValid();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the checksum of this record batch, which covers the batch header as well as all of the records.\n     *\n     * @return The 4-byte unsigned checksum represented as a long\n     */\n    long checksum();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the max timestamp or log append time of this record batch.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * If the timestamp type is create time, this is the max timestamp among all records contained in this batch and\n     * the value is updated during compaction. For log append time, this value is set by the broker and preserved during\n     * log compaction.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @return The max timestamp\n     */\n    long maxTimestamp();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the timestamp type of this record batch. This will be {@link TimestampType#NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE}\n     * if the batch has magic 0.\n     *\n     * @return The timestamp type\n     */\n    TimestampType timestampType();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the base offset contained in this record batch. For magic version prior to 2, the base offset will\n     * always be the offset of the first message in the batch. This generally requires deep iteration and will\n     * return the offset of the first record in the record batch. For magic version 2 and above, this will return\n     * the first offset of the original record batch (i.e. prior to compaction). For non-compacted topics, the\n     * behavior is equivalent.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * <strong>Performance Note:</strong> Because this requires deep iteration for older magic versions, this method\n     * should be used with caution. Generally {@link #lastOffset()} is safer since access is efficient for all magic versions.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @return The base offset of this record batch (which may or may not be the offset of the first record\n     *         as described above).\n     */\n    long baseOffset();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the last offset in this record batch (inclusive). Just like {@link #baseOffset()}, the last offset\n     * always reflects the offset of the last record in the original batch, even if it is removed during log\n     * compaction.\n     *\n     * @return The offset of the last record in this batch\n     */\n    long lastOffset();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the offset following this record batch (i.e. the last offset contained in this batch plus one).\n     *\n     * @return the next consecutive offset following this batch\n     */\n    long nextOffset();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the record format version of this record batch (i.e its magic value).\n     *\n     * @return the magic byte\n     */\n    byte magic();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the producer id for this log record batch. For older magic versions, this will return -1.\n     *\n     * @return The producer id, or {@link #NO_PRODUCER_ID} if there is none\n     */\n    long producerId();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the producer epoch for this log record batch.\n     *\n     * @return The producer epoch, or {@link #NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH} if there is none\n     */\n    short producerEpoch();\n\n    /**\n     * Does the batch have a valid producer id set.\n     *\n     * @return true if this batch has a valid producer id, false otherwise\n     */\n    boolean hasProducerId();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the base sequence number of this record batch. Like {@link #baseOffset()}, this value is not\n     * affected by compaction: it always retains the base sequence number from the original batch.\n     *\n     * @return The first sequence number or {@link #NO_SEQUENCE} if there is none\n     */\n    int baseSequence();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the last sequence number of this record batch. Like {@link #lastOffset()}, the last sequence number\n     * always reflects the sequence number of the last record in the original batch, even if it is removed during log\n     * compaction.\n     *\n     * @return The last sequence number or {@link #NO_SEQUENCE} if there is none\n     */\n    int lastSequence();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the compression type of this record batch.\n     *\n     * @return The compression type\n     */\n    CompressionType compressionType();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the size in bytes of this batch, including the size of the record and the batch overhead.\n     *\n     * @return The size in bytes of this batch\n     */\n    int sizeInBytes();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the count if it is efficiently supported by the record format (which is only the case\n     * for magic 2 and higher).\n     *\n     * @return The number of records in the batch, or null for magic versions 0 and 1.\n     */\n    Integer countOrNull();\n\n    /**\n     * Check whether this record batch is compressed.\n     *\n     * @return true if compressed, false otherwise\n     */\n    boolean isCompressed();\n\n    /**\n     * Write this record batch into a buffer.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to write the batch to\n     */\n    void writeTo(ByteBuffer buffer);\n\n    /**\n     * Whether or not this record batch is part of a transaction.\n     *\n     * @return true if it is transactional, false otherwise\n     */\n    boolean isTransactional();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the delete horizon, returns OptionalLong.EMPTY if the first timestamp is not the delete horizon.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * The delete horizon is used to mark when tombstones and transaction markers should be removed during log compaction.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @return timestamp of the delete horizon as OptionalLong\n     */\n    OptionalLong deleteHorizonMs();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the partition leader epoch of this record batch.\n     *\n     * @return The leader epoch or {@link #NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH} if it is unknown\n     */\n    int partitionLeaderEpoch();\n\n    /**\n     * Return a streaming iterator which basically delays decompression of the record stream until the records\n     * are actually asked for using {@link Iterator#next()}. If the message format does not support streaming\n     * iteration, then the normal iterator is returned. Either way, callers should ensure that the iterator is closed.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * <strong>Performance Note:</strong> For small record batches, allocating a potentially large buffer (64 KB for LZ4)\n     * will dominate the cost of decompressing and iterating over the records in the batch. As such, a supplier that reuses\n     * buffers will have a significant performance impact.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param decompressionBufferSupplier The supplier of ByteBuffer(s) used for decompression if supported.\n     * @return The closeable iterator for streaming over records in this batch\n     */\n    CloseableIterator<Record> streamingIterator(BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier);\n\n    /**\n     * Check whether this is a control batch (i.e. whether the control bit is set in the batch attributes).\n     * For magic versions prior to 2, this is always false.\n     *\n     * @return true if this batch contains control records, false otherwise\n     */\n    boolean isControlBatch();\n\n    /**\n     * Iterate all records to find the offset of max timestamp.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * Notes:\n     * <ul>\n     *   <li>The earliest offset will be returned if there are multiple records with the same (max) timestamp</li>\n     *   <li>It always returns an empty Optional if the {@link RecordBatch#magic()} is equal to {@link RecordBatch#MAGIC_VALUE_V0}</li>\n     * </ul>\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @return offset of max timestamp, or an empty Optional if not found or if magic is V0\n     */\n    default Optional<Long> offsetOfMaxTimestamp() {\n        if (magic() == RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V0) return Optional.empty();\n        long maxTimestamp = maxTimestamp();\n        try (CloseableIterator<Record> iter = streamingIterator(BufferSupplier.create())) {\n            while (iter.hasNext()) {\n                Record record = iter.next();\n                if (maxTimestamp == record.timestamp()) return Optional.of(record.offset());\n            }\n        }\n        return Optional.empty();\n    }\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":202,"cache_read_input_tokens":64399,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":202},"output_tokens":2,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"bedbdc7b-f047-4f3f-99d1-0bb86000f81b","uuid":"a140f9c9-fffd-4526-86ef-220d3ed51dd3"}

*\n     * @return The last sequence number or {@link #NO_SEQUENCE} if there is none\n     */\n    int lastSequence();\n\n    /**\n     * Get the compression type of this record batch.\n     *\n     * This class handles the serialization and\n * deserialization of record batches in the Kafka wire format.\n *\n * <p>\n * The binary schema for a magic v2 record batch is:\n * <pre>\n * RecordBatch =>\n *  BaseOffset => Int64\n *  Length => Int32\n *  PartitionLeaderEpoch => Int32\n *  Magic => Int8\n *  CRC => Uint32\n *  Attributes => Int16\n *  LastOffsetDelta => Int32 // also serves as LastSequenceDelta\n *  BaseTimestamp => Int64\n *  MaxTimestamp => Int64\n *  ProducerId => Int64\n *  ProducerEpoch => Int16\n *  BaseSequence => Int32\n *  RecordsCount => Int32\n *  Records => [Record]\n * </pre>\n * </p>\n *\n * <p>\n * <strong>Thread Safety:</strong> This class is NOT thread-safe. The underlying ByteBuffer may be modified\n * by operations like {@link #setMaxTimestamp(TimestampType, long)}, {@link #setPartitionLeaderEpoch(int)},\n * and {@link #setLastOffset(long)}. Callers must ensure external synchronization if shared across threads.\n * </p>\n *\n * <p>\n * <strong>Key Implementation Details:</strong>\n * <ul>\n *   <li>The CRC covers the data from the attributes to the end of the batch (i.e. all the bytes that follow the CRC).\n *       The partition leader epoch field is not included in the CRC computation.</li>\n *   <li>On Compaction: Unlike older message formats, magic v2 preserves the first and last offset/sequence numbers\n *       from the original batch when the log is cleaned. This is required to restore the producer's state.</li>\n *   <li>Empty batches may be retained to preserve producer sequence information until a new sequence number is written\n *       by the producer or the producer ID expires.</li>\n *   <li>The BaseTimestamp field reflects the timestamp of the first record in the batch in most cases.\n *       If the batch is empty, it is set to -1 (NO_TIMESTAMP). If the delete horizon flag is set, it is set to the\n *       time at which tombstone records and aborted transaction markers should be removed.</li>\n *   <li>The MaxTimestamp field reflects the maximum timestamp of the current records if the timestamp type is CREATE_TIME.\n *       For LOG_APPEND_TIME, it reflects the timestamp set by the broker and is preserved after compaction.</li>\n * </ul>\n * </p>\n *\n * @see RecordBatch for the interface\n * @see MemoryRecords for managing collections of record batches\n * @see MemoryRecordsBuilder for building new record batches\n */\npublic class DefaultRecordBatch extends AbstractRecordBatch implements MutableRecordBatch {\n    static final int BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET = 0;\n    static final int BASE_OFFSET_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int LENGTH_OFFSET = BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET + BASE_OFFSET_LENGTH;\n    static final int LENGTH_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET = LENGTH_OFFSET + LENGTH_LENGTH;\n    static final int PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int MAGIC_OFFSET = PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET + PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_LENGTH;\n    static final int MAGIC_LENGTH = 1;\n    public static final int CRC_OFFSET = MAGIC_OFFSET + MAGIC_LENGTH;\n    static final int CRC_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET = CRC_OFFSET + CRC_LENGTH;\n    static final int ATTRIBUTE_LENGTH = 2;\n    public static final int LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_OFFSET = ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET + ATTRIBUTE_LENGTH;\n    static final int LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET = LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_OFFSET + LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_LENGTH;\n    static final int BASE_TIMESTAMP_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET = BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET + BASE_TIMESTAMP_LENGTH;\n    static final int MAX_TIMESTAMP_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int PRODUCER_ID_OFFSET = MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET + MAX_TIMESTAMP_LENGTH;\n    static final int PRODUCER_ID_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int PRODUCER_EPOCH_OFFSET = PRODUCER_ID_OFFSET + PRODUCER_ID_LENGTH;\n    static final int PRODUCER_EPOCH_LENGTH = 2;\n    static final int BASE_SEQUENCE_OFFSET = PRODUCER_EPOCH_OFFSET + PRODUCER_EPOCH_LENGTH;\n    static final int BASE_SEQUENCE_LENGTH = 4;\n    public static final int RECORDS_COUNT_OFFSET = BASE_SEQUENCE_OFFSET + BASE_SEQUENCE_LENGTH;\n    static final int RECORDS_COUNT_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int RECORDS_OFFSET = RECORDS_COUNT_OFFSET + RECORDS_COUNT_LENGTH;\n    public static final int RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD = RECORDS_OFFSET;\n\n    private static final byte COMPRESSION_CODEC_MASK = 0x07;\n    private static final byte TRANSACTIONAL_FLAG_MASK = 0x10;\n    private static final int CONTROL_FLAG_MASK = 0x20;\n    private static final byte DELETE_HORIZON_FLAG_MASK = 0x40;\n    private static final byte TIMESTAMP_TYPE_MASK = 0x08;\n\n    private final ByteBuffer buffer;\n\n    /**\n     * Construct a DefaultRecordBatch from a ByteBuffer.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * The buffer should contain a complete magic v2 record batch starting at position 0.\n     * The buffer's limit should be set to the end of the batch data.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param buffer The ByteBuffer containing the batch data. The buffer is not copied;\n     *               the constructed batch maintains a reference to it.\n     */\n    DefaultRecordBatch(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        this.buffer = buffer;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public byte magic() {\n        return buffer.get(MAGIC_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void ensureValid() {\n        if (sizeInBytes() < RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD)\n            throw new CorruptRecordException(\"Record batch is corrupt (the size \" + sizeInBytes() +\n                    \" is smaller than the minimum allowed overhead \" + RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD + \")\");\n\n        if (!isValid())\n            throw new CorruptRecordException(\"Record is corrupt (stored crc = \" + checksum()\n                    + \", computed crc = \" + computeChecksum() + \")\");\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Gets the base timestamp of the batch which is used to calculate the record timestamps from the deltas.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * The base timestamp is the timestamp of the first record in the batch, unless the batch is empty or\n     * the delete horizon flag is set, in which case it may be set to NO_TIMESTAMP or the delete horizon time.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @return The base timestamp\n     */\n    public long baseTimestamp() {\n        return buffer.getLong(BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long maxTimestamp() {\n        return buffer.getLong(MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public TimestampType timestampType() {\n        return (attributes() & TIMESTAMP_TYPE_MASK) == 0 ? TimestampType.CREATE_TIME : TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long baseOffset() {\n        return buffer.getLong(BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long lastOffset() {\n        return baseOffset() + lastOffsetDelta();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long producerId() {\n        return buffer.getLong(PRODUCER_ID_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public short producerEpoch() {\n        return buffer.getShort(PRODUCER_EPOCH_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int baseSequence() {\n        return buffer.getInt(BASE_SEQUENCE_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    private int lastOffsetDelta() {\n        return buffer.getInt(LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int lastSequence() {\n        int baseSequence = baseSequence();\n        if (baseSequence == RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE)\n            return RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE;\n        return incrementSequence(baseSequence, lastOffsetDelta());\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public CompressionType compressionType() {\n        return CompressionType.forId(attributes() & COMPRESSION_CODEC_MASK);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int sizeInBytes() {\n        return LOG_OVERHEAD + buffer.getInt(LENGTH_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    private int count() {\n        return buffer.getInt(RECORDS_COUNT_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Integer countOrNull() {\n        return count();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void writeTo(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        buffer.put(this.buffer.duplicate());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Write this record batch to a ByteBufferOutputStream.\n     *\n     * @param outputStream The output stream to write the batch to\n     */\n    public void writeTo(ByteBufferOutputStream outputStream) {\n        outputStream.write(this.buffer.duplicate());\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean isTransactional() {\n        return (attributes() & TRANSACTIONAL_FLAG_MASK) > 0;\n    }\n\n    private boolean hasDeleteHorizonMs() {\n        return (attributes() & DELETE_HORIZON_FLAG_MASK) > 0;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public OptionalLong deleteHorizonMs() {\n        if (hasDeleteHorizonMs())\n            return OptionalLong.of(buffer.getLong(BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET));\n        else\n            return OptionalLong.empty();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean isControlBatch() {\n        return (attributes() & CONTROL_FLAG_MASK) > 0;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int partitionLeaderEpoch() {\n        return buffer.getInt(PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Returns an InputStream for reading the record data from this batch.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * <strong>Performance Note:</strong> If the batch is compressed, the returned InputStream will decompress\n     * the data on-the-fly as it is read. Decompression performance depends on the compression type and can be\n     * optimized by providing a buffer supplier that reuses buffers.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param bufferSupplier The supplier of ByteBuffer(s) used for decompression if needed\n     * @return An InputStream positioned at the start of the record data\n     */\n    public InputStream recordInputStream(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier) {\n        final ByteBuffer buffer = this.buffer.duplicate();\n        buffer.position(RECORDS_OFFSET);\n        return Compression.of(compressionType()).build().wrapForInput(buffer, magic(), bufferSupplier);\n    }\n\n    private CloseableIterator<Record> compressedIterator(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier, boolean skipKeyValue) {\n        final InputStream inputStream = recordInputStream(bufferSupplier);\n\n        if (skipKeyValue) {\n            return new StreamRecordIterator(inputStream) {\n                @Override\n                protected Record doReadRecord(long baseOffset, long baseTimestamp, int baseSequence, Long logAppendTime) throws IOException {\n                    return DefaultRecord.readPartiallyFrom(inputStream, baseOffset, baseTimestamp, baseSequence, logAppendTime);\n                }\n            };\n        } else {\n            return new StreamRecordIterator(inputStream) {\n                @Override\n                protected Record doReadRecord(long baseOffset, long baseTimestamp, int baseSequence, Long logAppendTime) throws IOException {\n                    return DefaultRecord.readFrom(inputStream, baseOffset, baseTimestamp, baseSequence, logAppendTime);\n                }\n            };\n        }\n    }\n\n    private CloseableIterator<Record> uncompressedIterator() {\n        final ByteBuffer buffer = this.buffer.duplicate();\n        buffer.position(RECORDS_OFFSET);\n        return new RecordIterator() {\n            @Override\n            protected Record readNext(long baseOffset, long baseTimestamp, int baseSequence, Long logAppendTime) {\n                try {\n                    return DefaultRecord.readFrom(buffer, baseOffset, baseTimestamp, baseSequence, logAppendTime);\n                } catch (BufferUnderflowException e) {\n                    throw new InvalidRecordException(\"Incorrect declared batch size, premature EOF reached\");\n                }\n            }\n            @Override\n            protected boolean ensureNoneRemaining() {\n                return !buffer.hasRemaining();\n            }\n            @Override\n            public void close() {}\n        };\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Iterator<Record> iterator() {\n        if (count() == 0)\n            return Collections.emptyIterator();\n\n        if (!isCompressed())\n            return uncompressedIterator();\n\n        // for a normal iterator, we cannot ensure that the underlying compression stream is closed,\n        // so we decompress the full record set here. Use cases which call for a lower memory footprint\n        // can use `streamingIterator` at the cost of additional complexity\n        try (CloseableIterator<Record> iterator = compressedIterator(BufferSupplier.NO_CACHING, false)) {\n            List<Record> records = new ArrayList<>(count());\n            while (iterator.hasNext())\n                records.add(iterator.next());\n            return records.iterator();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Returns a closeable iterator that skips over the key, value, and headers of records.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * <strong>Performance Note:</strong> This method is used for validation purposes where the record contents\n     * are not needed. For uncompressed batches, this may not provide a performance benefit over\n     * {@link #iterator()} since the ByteBuffer's skip operation is less efficient than reading.\n     * For compressed batches, a buffer supplier can significantly improve performance.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param bufferSupplier The supplier of ByteBuffer(s) used for decompression if needed\n     * @return A closeable iterator that skips key, value, and headers\n     */\n    public CloseableIterator<Record> skipKeyValueIterator(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier) {\n        if (count() == 0) {\n            return CloseableIterator.wrap(Collections.emptyIterator());\n        }\n\n        /*\n         * For uncompressed iterator, it is actually not worth skipping key / value / headers at all since\n         * its ByteBufferInputStream's skip() function is less efficient compared with just reading it actually\n         * as it will allocate new byte array.\n         */\n        if (!isCompressed())\n            return uncompressedIterator();\n\n        // we define this to be a closable iterator so that caller (i.e. the log validator) needs to close it\n        // while we can save memory footprint of not decompressing the full record set ahead of time\n        return compressedIterator(bufferSupplier, true);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public CloseableIterator<Record> streamingIterator(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier) {\n        if (isCompressed())\n            return compressedIterator(bufferSupplier, false);\n        else\n            return uncompressedIterator();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Set the base offset of this batch.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * This method updates the underlying buffer's base offset field to ensure the last offset\n     * (calculated as baseOffset + lastOffsetDelta) matches the provided offset.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param offset The new base offset (the last offset is maintained by adjusting the base offset)\n     */\n    public void setLastOffset(long offset) {\n        buffer.putLong(BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET, offset - lastOffsetDelta());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Set the max timestamp and potentially update the timestamp type for this batch.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * This method updates both the max timestamp and the timestamp type attributes, then recomputes the CRC\n     * to ensure batch integrity. If the timestamp type and max timestamp are already as specified,\n     * no changes are made to avoid unnecessary CRC recomputation.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param timestampType The timestamp type (CREATE_TIME or LOG_APPEND_TIME)\n     * @param maxTimestamp The new max timestamp\n     */\n    public void setMaxTimestamp(TimestampType timestampType, long maxTimestamp) {\n        long currentMaxTimestamp = maxTimestamp();\n        // We don't need to recompute crc if the timestamp is not updated.\n        if (timestampType() == timestampType && currentMaxTimestamp == maxTimestamp)\n            return;\n\n        byte attributes = computeAttributes(compressionType(), timestampType, isTransactional(), isControlBatch(), hasDeleteHorizonMs());\n        buffer.putShort(ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, attributes);\n        buffer.putLong(MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET, maxTimestamp);\n        long crc = computeChecksum();\n        ByteUtils.writeUnsignedInt(buffer, CRC_OFFSET, crc);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Set the partition leader epoch for this batch.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * Note that the partition leader epoch is not included in the CRC computation,\n     * so this method does not require CRC recomputation.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param epoch The new partition leader epoch\n     */\n    public void setPartitionLeaderEpoch(int epoch) {\n        buffer.putInt(PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET, epoch);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long checksum() {\n        return ByteUtils.readUnsignedInt(buffer, CRC_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Verify that the checksum of this batch is valid.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * This method compares the stored CRC with the computed CRC, accounting for minimum size requirements.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @return true if the batch size is valid and the checksum matches, false otherwise\n     */\n    public boolean isValid() {\n        return sizeInBytes() >= RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD && checksum() == computeChecksum();\n    }\n\n    private long computeChecksum() {\n        return Crc32C.compute(buffer, ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, buffer.limit() - ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    private byte attributes() {\n        // note we're not using the second byte of attributes\n        return (byte) buffer.getShort(ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean equals(Object o) {\n        if (this == o)\n            return true;\n        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass())\n            return false;\n\n        DefaultRecordBatch that = (DefaultRecordBatch) o;\n        return Objects.equals(buffer, that.buffer);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int hashCode() {\n        return buffer != null ? buffer.hashCode() : 0;\n    }\n\n    private static byte computeAttributes(CompressionType type, TimestampType timestampType,\n                                          boolean isTransactional, boolean isControl, boolean isDeleteHorizonSet) {\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Timestamp type must be provided to compute attributes for message \" +\n                    \"format v2 and above\");\n\n        byte attributes = isTransactional ? TRANSACTIONAL_FLAG_MASK : 0;\n        if (isControl)\n            attributes |= CONTROL_FLAG_MASK;\n        if (type.id > 0)\n            attributes |= (byte) (COMPRESSION_CODEC_MASK & type.id);\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME)\n            attributes |= TIMESTAMP_TYPE_MASK;\n        if (isDeleteHorizonSet)\n            attributes |= DELETE_HORIZON_FLAG_MASK;\n        return attributes;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Write an empty record batch header to the provided buffer.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * An empty batch is used to preserve producer sequence information during log compaction.\n     * The batch contains no records but retains all the header information.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to write to\n     * @param magic The magic version\n     * @param producerId The producer ID\n     * @param producerEpoch The producer epoch\n     * @param baseSequence The base sequence number\n     * @param baseOffset The base offset\n     * @param lastOffset The last offset (inclusive)\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The partition leader epoch\n     * @param timestampType The timestamp type\n     * @param timestamp The timestamp value\n     * @param isTransactional Whether this is a transactional batch\n     * @param isControlRecord Whether this is a control batch\n     */\n    public static void writeEmptyHeader(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                        byte magic,\n                                        long producerId,\n                                        short producerEpoch,\n                                        int baseSequence,\n                                        long baseOffset,\n                                        long lastOffset,\n                                        int partitionLeaderEpoch,\n                                        TimestampType timestampType,\n                                        long timestamp,\n                                        boolean isTransactional,\n                                        boolean isControlRecord) {\n        int offsetDelta = (int) (lastOffset - baseOffset);\n        writeHeader(buffer, baseOffset, offsetDelta, DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD, magic,\n                    CompressionType.NONE, timestampType, RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP, timestamp, producerId,\n                    producerEpoch, baseSequence, isTransactional, isControlRecord, false, partitionLeaderEpoch, 0);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Write a complete record batch header to the provided buffer.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * <strong>Performance Note:</strong> This method performs CRC computation, which involves reading and\n     * hashing the batch data. For large batches, this can be a significant operation.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to write to\n     * @param baseOffset The base offset\n     * @param lastOffsetDelta The last offset delta (last offset - base offset)\n     * @param sizeInBytes The total size of the batch in bytes (including overhead)\n     * @param magic The magic version\n     * @param compressionType The compression type\n     * @param timestampType The timestamp type\n     * @param baseTimestamp The base timestamp\n     * @param maxTimestamp The max timestamp\n     * @param producerId The producer ID\n     * @param epoch The producer epoch\n     * @param sequence The base sequence number\n     * @param isTransactional Whether this is a transactional batch\n     * @param isControlBatch Whether this is a control batch\n     * @param isDeleteHorizonSet Whether the delete horizon flag is set\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The partition leader epoch\n     * @param numRecords The number of records in the batch\n     * @throws IllegalArgumentException if the magic value or timestamp is invalid\n     */\n    public static void writeHeader(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                   long baseOffset,\n                                   int lastOffsetDelta,\n                                   int sizeInBytes,\n                                   byte magic,\n                                   CompressionType compressionType,\n                                   TimestampType timestampType,\n                                   long baseTimestamp,\n                                   long maxTimestamp,\n                                   long producerId,\n                                   short epoch,\n                                   int sequence,\n                                   boolean isTransactional,\n                                   boolean isControlBatch,\n                                   boolean isDeleteHorizonSet,\n                                   int partitionLeaderEpoch,\n                                   int numRecords) {\n        if (magic < RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid magic value \" + magic);\n        if (baseTimestamp < 0 && baseTimestamp != NO_TIMESTAMP)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid message timestamp \" + baseTimestamp);\n\n        short attributes = computeAttributes(compressionType, timestampType, isTransactional, isControlBatch, isDeleteHorizonSet);\n\n        int position = buffer.position();\n        buffer.putLong(position + BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET, baseOffset);\n        buffer.putInt(position + LENGTH_OFFSET, sizeInBytes - LOG_OVERHEAD);\n        buffer.putInt(position + PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET, partitionLeaderEpoch);\n        buffer.put(position + MAGIC_OFFSET, magic);\n        buffer.putShort(position + ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, attributes);\n        buffer.putLong(position + BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET, baseTimestamp);\n        buffer.putLong(position + MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET, maxTimestamp);\n        buffer.putInt(position + LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_OFFSET, lastOffsetDelta);\n        buffer.putLong(position + PRODUCER_ID_OFFSET, producerId);\n        buffer.putShort(position + PRODUCER_EPOCH_OFFSET, epoch);\n        buffer.putInt(position + BASE_SEQUENCE_OFFSET, sequence);\n        buffer.putInt(position + RECORDS_COUNT_OFFSET, numRecords);\n        long crc = Crc32C.compute(buffer, ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, sizeInBytes - ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET);\n        buffer.putInt(position + CRC_OFFSET, (int) crc);\n        buffer.position(position + RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return \"RecordBatch(magic=\" + magic() + \", offsets=[\" + baseOffset() + \", \" + lastOffset() + \"], \" +\n                \"sequence=[\" + baseSequence() + \", \" + lastSequence() + \"], \" +\n                \"partitionLeaderEpoch=\" + partitionLeaderEpoch() + \", \" +\n This class handles the serialization and\n * deserialization of record batches in the Kafka wire format.\n *\n * <p>\n * The binary schema for a magic v2 record batch is:\n * <pre>\n * RecordBatch =>\n *  BaseOffset => Int64\n *  Length => Int32\n *  PartitionLeaderEpoch => Int32\n *  Magic => Int8\n *  CRC => Uint32\n *  Attributes => Int16\n *  LastOffsetDelta => Int32 // also serves as LastSequenceDelta\n *  BaseTimestamp => Int64\n *  MaxTimestamp => Int64\n *  ProducerId => Int64\n *  ProducerEpoch => Int16\n *  BaseSequence => Int32\n *  RecordsCount => Int32\n *  Records => [Record]\n * </pre>\n * </p>\n *\n * <p>\n * <strong>Thread Safety:</strong> This class is NOT thread-safe. The underlying ByteBuffer may be modified\n * by operations like {@link #setMaxTimestamp(TimestampType, long)}, {@link #setPartitionLeaderEpoch(int)},\n * and {@link #setLastOffset(long)}. Callers must ensure external synchronization if shared across threads.\n * </p>\n *\n * <p>\n * <strong>Key Implementation Details:</strong>\n * <ul>\n *   <li>The CRC covers the data from the attributes to the end of the batch (i.e. all the bytes that follow the CRC).\n *       The partition leader epoch field is not included in the CRC computation.</li>\n *   <li>On Compaction: Unlike older message formats, magic v2 preserves the first and last offset/sequence numbers\n *       from the original batch when the log is cleaned. This is required to restore the producer's state.</li>\n *   <li>Empty batches may be retained to preserve producer sequence information until a new sequence number is written\n *       by the producer or the producer ID expires.</li>\n *   <li>The BaseTimestamp field reflects the timestamp of the first record in the batch in most cases.\n *       If the batch is empty, it is set to -1 (NO_TIMESTAMP). If the delete horizon flag is set, it is set to the\n *       time at which tombstone records and aborted transaction markers should be removed.</li>\n *   <li>The MaxTimestamp field reflects the maximum timestamp of the current records if the timestamp type is CREATE_TIME.\n *       For LOG_APPEND_TIME, it reflects the timestamp set by the broker and is preserved after compaction.</li>\n * </ul>\n * </p>\n *\n * @see RecordBatch for the interface\n * @see MemoryRecords for managing collections of record batches\n * @see MemoryRecordsBuilder for building new record batches\n */\npublic class DefaultRecordBatch extends AbstractRecordBatch implements MutableRecordBatch {\n    static final int BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET = 0;\n    static final int BASE_OFFSET_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int LENGTH_OFFSET = BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET + BASE_OFFSET_LENGTH;\n    static final int LENGTH_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET = LENGTH_OFFSET + LENGTH_LENGTH;\n    static final int PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int MAGIC_OFFSET = PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET + PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_LENGTH;\n    static final int MAGIC_LENGTH = 1;\n    public static final int CRC_OFFSET = MAGIC_OFFSET + MAGIC_LENGTH;\n    static final int CRC_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET = CRC_OFFSET + CRC_LENGTH;\n    static final int ATTRIBUTE_LENGTH = 2;\n    public static final int LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_OFFSET = ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET + ATTRIBUTE_LENGTH;\n    static final int LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_LENGTH = 4;\n    static final int BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET = LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_OFFSET + LAST_OFFSET_DELTA_LENGTH;\n    static final int BASE_TIMESTAMP_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET = BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET + BASE_TIMESTAMP_LENGTH;\n    static final int MAX_TIMESTAMP_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int PRODUCER_ID_OFFSET = MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET + MAX_TIMESTAMP_LENGTH;\n    static final int PRODUCER_ID_LENGTH = 8;\n    static final int DELETE_HORIZON_FLAG_MASK = 0x40;\n    private static final byte TIMESTAMP_TYPE_MASK = 0x08;\n\n    private final ByteBuffer buffer;\n\n    /**\n     * Construct a DefaultRecordBatch from a ByteBuffer.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * The buffer should contain a complete magic v2 record batch starting at position 0.\n     * The buffer's limit should be set to the end of the batch data.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param buffer The ByteBuffer containing the batch data. The buffer is not copied;\n     *               the constructed batch maintains a reference to it.\n     */\n    DefaultRecordBatch(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        this.buffer = buffer;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public byte magic() {\n        return buffer.get(MAGIC_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void ensureValid() {\n        if (sizeInBytes() < RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD)\n            throw new CorruptRecordException(\"Record batch is corrupt (the size \" + sizeInBytes() +\n                    \" is smaller than the minimum allowed overhead \" + RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD + \")\");\n\n        if (!isValid())\n            throw new CorruptRecordException(\"Record is corrupt (stored crc = \" + checksum()\n                    + \", computed crc = \" + computeChecksum() + \")\");\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Gets the base timestamp of the batch which is used to calculate the record timestamps from the deltas.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * The base timestamp is the timestamp of the first record in the batch, unless the batch is empty or\n     * the delete horizon flag is set, in which case it may be set to NO_TIMESTAMP or the delete horizon time.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @return The base timestamp\n     */\n    public long baseTimestamp() {\n        return buffer.getLong(BASE_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long maxTimestamp() {\n        return buffer.getLong(MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public TimestampType timestampType() {\n        return (attributes() & TIMESTAMP_TYPE_MASK) == 0 ? TimestampType.CREATE_TIME : TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long baseOffset() {\n        return buffer.getLong(BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n      int baseSequence = baseSequence();\n        if (baseSequence == RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE)\n            return RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE;\n        return incrementSequence(baseSequence, lastOffsetDelta());\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public CompressionType compressionType() {\n        return CompressionType.forId(attributes() & COMPRESSION_CODEC_MASK);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int sizeInBytes() {\n        return LOG_OVERHEAD + buffer.getInt(LENGTH_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    private int count() {\n        return buffer.getInt(RECORDS_COUNT_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Integer countOrNull() {\n        return count();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void writeTo(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        buffer.put(this.buffer.duplicate());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Write this record batch to a ByteBufferOutputStream.\n     *\n     * @param outputStream The output stream to write the batch to\n     */\n    public void writeTo(ByteBufferOutputStream }\n\n    private boolean hasDeleteHorizonMs() {\n        return (attributes() & DELETE_HORIZON_FLAG_MASK) > 0;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public OptionalLong deleteHorizonMs() {\n        if buffer.getInt(PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Returns an InputStream for reading the record data from this batch.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * <strong>Performance Note:</strong> If the batch is compressed, the returned InputStream will decompress\n     * the data on-the-fly as it is read. Decompression performance depends on the compression type and can be\n     * optimized by providing a buffer supplier that reuses buffers.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param bufferSupplier The bufferSupplier) {\n        final ByteBuffer buffer = this.buffer.duplicate();\n        buffer.position(RECORDS_OFFSET);\n        return Compression.of(compressionType()).build().wrapForInput(buffer, magic(), bufferSupplier);\n    }\n\n    private CloseableIterator<Record> compressedIterator(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier, boolean skipKeyValue) {\n        final InputStream inputStream = recordInputStream(bufferSupplier);\n\n        if (skipKeyValue) {\n            return new StreamRecordIterator(inputStream) {\n                @Override\n                protected Record doReadRecord(long baseOffset, long baseTimestamp, int baseSequence, Long logAppendTime) throws IOException {\n                    return DefaultRecord.readPartiallyFrom(inputStream, baseOffset, baseTimestamp, baseSequence, logAppendTime);\n                }\n            };\n        } else {\n            return new StreamRecordIterator(inputStream) {\n                @Override\n                protected Record doReadRecord(long baseOffset, long baseTimestamp, int baseSequence, Long logAppendTime) throws IOException {\n                    return DefaultRecord.readFrom(inputStream, baseOffset, baseTimestamp, baseSequence, logAppendTime);\n                }\n            };\n        }\n    }\n\n    private CloseableIterator<Record> uncompressedIterator() {\n        final ByteBuffer buffer = this.buffer.duplicate();\n        buffer.position(RECORDS_OFFSET);\n        return new RecordIterator() {\n            @Override\n            protected Record readNext(long baseOffset, long baseTimestamp, int baseSequence, Long logAppendTime) {\n                try {\n                    return DefaultRecord.readFrom(buffer, baseOffset, baseTimestamp, baseSequence, logAppendTime);\n                } catch (BufferUnderflowException e) {\n                    throw new InvalidRecordException(\"Incorrect declared batch size, premature EOF reached\");\n                }\n            }\n            @Override\n            protected boolean ensureNoneRemaining() {\n                return !buffer.hasRemaining();\n            }\n            @Override\n            public void close() {}\n        };\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Iterator<Record> iterator() {\n        if (count() == 0)\n            return Collections.emptyIterator();\n\n        if (!isCompressed())\n            return uncompressedIterator();\n\n        // for a normal iterator, we cannot ensure that the underlying compression stream is closed,\n        // so we decompress the full record set here. Use cases which call for a lower memory footprint\n        // can use `streamingIterator` at the cost of additional complexity\n        try (CloseableIterator<Record> iterator = compressedIterator(BufferSupplier.NO_CACHING, false)) {\n            List<Record> records = new ArrayList<>(count());\n            while (iterator.hasNext())\n                records.add(iterator.next());\n            return records.iterator();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Returns a closeable iterator that skips over the key, value, and headers of records.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * <strong>Performance Note:</strong> This method is used for validation purposes where the record contents\n     * are not needed. For uncompressed batches, this may not provide a performance benefit over\n     * {@link #iterator()} since the ByteBuffer's skip operation is less efficient than reading.\n     * For compressed batches, a buffer supplier can significantly improve performance.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param bufferSupplier The supplier of ByteBuffer(s) used for decompression if needed\n     * @return A closeable iterator that skips key, value, and headers\n     */\n    public CloseableIterator<Record> skipKeyValueIterator(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier) {\n        if (count() == 0) {\n            return CloseableIterator.wrap(Collections.emptyIterator());\n        }\n\n        /*\n         * For uncompressed iterator, it is actually not worth skipping key / value / headers at all since\n         * its ByteBufferInputStream's skip() function is less efficient compared with just reading it actually\n         * as it will allocate new byte array.\n         */\n        if (!isCompressed())\n            return uncompressedIterator();\n\n        // we define this to be a closable iterator so that caller (i.e. the log validator) needs to close it\n        // while we can save memory footprint of not decompressing the full record set ahead of time\n        return compressedIterator(bufferSupplier, true);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public CloseableIterator<Record> streamingIterator(BufferSupplier bufferSupplier) {\n        if (isCompressed())\n            return compressedIterator(bufferSupplier, false);\n        else\n            return uncompressedIterator();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Set the base offset of this batch.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * This method updates the underlying buffer's base offset field to ensure the last offset\n     * (calculated as baseOffset + lastOffsetDelta) matches the provided offset.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param offset The new base offset (the last offset is maintained by adjusting the base offset)\n     */\n    public void setLastOffset(long offset) {\n        buffer.putLong(BASE_OFFSET_OFFSET, offset - lastOffsetDelta());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Set the max timestamp and potentially update the timestamp type for this batch.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * This method updates both the max timestamp and the timestamp type attributes, then recomputes the CRC\n     * to ensure batch integrity. If the timestamp type and max timestamp are already as specified,\n     * no changes are made to avoid unnecessary CRC recomputation.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param timestampType The timestamp type (CREATE_TIME or LOG_APPEND_TIME)\n     * @param maxTimestamp The new max timestamp\n     */\n    public void setMaxTimestamp(TimestampType timestampType, long maxTimestamp) {\n        long currentMaxTimestamp = maxTimestamp();\n        // We don't need to recompute crc if the timestamp is not updated.\n        if (timestampType() == timestampType && currentMaxTimestamp == maxTimestamp)\n            return;\n\n        byte attributes = computeAttributes(compressionType(), timestampType, isTransactional(), isControlBatch(), hasDeleteHorizonMs());\n        buffer.putShort(ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, attributes);\n        buffer.putLong(MAX_TIMESTAMP_OFFSET, maxTimestamp);\n        long crc = computeChecksum();\n        ByteUtils.writeUnsignedInt(buffer, CRC_OFFSET, crc);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Set the partition leader epoch for this batch.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * Note that the partition leader epoch is not included in the CRC computation,\n     * so this method does not require CRC recomputation.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param epoch The new partition leader epoch\n     */\n    public void setPartitionLeaderEpoch(int epoch) {\n        buffer.putInt(PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH_OFFSET, epoch);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public long checksum() {\n        return ByteUtils.readUnsignedInt(buffer, CRC_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Verify that the checksum of this batch is valid.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * This method compares the stored CRC with the computed CRC, accounting for minimum size requirements.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @return true if the batch size is valid and the checksum matches, false otherwise\n     */\n    public boolean isValid() {\n        return sizeInBytes() >= RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD && checksum() == computeChecksum();\n    }\n\n    private long computeChecksum() {\n        return Crc32C.compute(buffer, ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET, buffer.limit() - ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    private byte attributes() {\n        // note we're not using the second byte of attributes\n        return (byte) buffer.getShort(ATTRIBUTES_OFFSET);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean equals(Object o) {\n        if (this == o)\n            return true;\n        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass())\n            return false;\n\n        DefaultRecordBatch that = (DefaultRecordBatch) o;\n        return Objects.equals(buffer, that.buffer);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int hashCode() {\n        return buffer != null ? buffer.hashCode() : 0;\n    }\n\n    private static byte (timestampType == TimestampType.NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Timestamp type must be provided to compute attributes for message \" +\n                    \"format v2 and above\");\n\n        byte attributes = isTransactional ?                      int baseSequence,\n                                        long baseOffset,\n                                        long lastOffset,\n                                        int baseSequence, isTransactional, isControlRecord, false, partitionLeaderEpoch, 0);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Write a complete record batch header to the provided buffer.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * The compression type\n     * @param timestampType The timestamp type\n     * @param baseTimestamp The base timestamp\n     * @param maxTimestamp The max timestamp\n     * @param producerId The Whether this is a control batch\n     * @param isDeleteHorizonSet Whether the delete horizon flag is set\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The partition leader epoch\n     * @param numRecords The               long baseOffset,\n                                   int lastOffsetDelta,\n                                   int sizeInBytes,\n                                   byte magic,\n                                   CompressionType compressionType,\n                                   TimestampType timestampType,\n                                   long baseTimestamp,\n                                   long maxTimestamp,\n                                   long producerId,\n                                   short epoch,\n                                   int sequence,\n                                   boolean isTransactional,\n                                   boolean isControlBatch,\n                                   boolean isDeleteHorizonSet,\n                                   int partitionLeaderEpoch,\n                                   int numRecords) {\n        if (magic < RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid magic       return increment - (Integer.MAX_VALUE - sequence) - 1;\n        return sequence + increment;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Decrement a sequence number by the given amount, handling wraparound at This is used for reading and\n * in-place modification of existing record batches. To create new record batches, use\n * {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} or the {@link #builder(ByteBuffer, Compression, TimestampType, long)} static factory methods.\n *\n * <p>\n * <strong>Thread Safety:</strong> This class is NOT thread-safe. The underlying ByteBuffer may be modified\n * by filtering operations and other mutations. Callers must ensure external synchronization if shared across threads.\n * </p>\n *\n * <p>\n * <strong>Memory Model:</strong> MemoryRecords maintains a reference to a ByteBuffer but does not copy it.\n * Multiple MemoryRecords instances can be created from the same buffer (via {@link #slice(int, int)}),\n * and they will share the underlying data.\n * </p>\n *\n * @see DefaultRecordBatch for the batch format implementation\n * @see MemoryRecordsBuilder for building new MemoryRecords\n * @see Records for the parent interface\n */\npublic class MemoryRecords extends AbstractRecords {\n    /**\n     * An empty MemoryRecords instance backed by an empty buffer.\n     */\n    public static final MemoryRecords EMPTY = MemoryRecords.readableRecords(ByteBuffer.allocate(0));\n\n    private final ByteBuffer buffer;\n\n    private final Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches = this::batchIterator;\n\n    private int validBytes = -1;\n\n    /**\n     * Construct a MemoryRecords from a ByteBuffer.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * The buffer should contain one or more record batches. The buffer's position and limit\n     * define the region of valid data. The buffer is not copied; a reference to it is maintained.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param buffer The ByteBuffer containing record batch data. Must not be null.\n     * @throws NullPointerException if buffer is null\n     */\n    private MemoryRecords(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        Objects.requireNonNull(buffer, \"buffer should not be null\");\n        this.buffer = buffer;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int sizeInBytes() {\n        return buffer.limit();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int writeTo(TransferableChannel channel, int position, int length) throws IOException {\n        if (((long) position) + length > buffer.limit())\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"position+length should not be greater than buffer.limit(), position: \"\n                    + position + \", length: \" + length + \", buffer.limit(): \" + buffer.limit());\n\n        return Utils.tryWriteTo(channel, position, length, buffer);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Write all records to the given channel (including partial records).\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * This method writes the entire buffer contents to the channel, including any partial batches\n     * at the end. It resets the buffer's position after writing completes.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param channel The channel to write to\n     * @return The number of bytes written\n     * @throws IOException For any IO errors writing to the channel\n     */\n    public int writeFullyTo(GatheringByteChannel channel) throws IOException {\n        buffer.mark();\n        int written = 0;\n        while (written < sizeInBytes())\n            written += channel.write(buffer);\n        buffer.reset();\n        return written;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * The total number of bytes in this message set not including any partial, trailing messages. Subsequent calls return\n     * the cached value unless the MemoryRecords is modified.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @return The number of valid bytes (complete batches only)\n     */\n    public int validBytes() {\n        if (validBytes >= 0)\n            return validBytes;\n\n        int bytes = 0;\n        for (RecordBatch batch : batches())\n            bytes += batch.sizeInBytes();\n\n        this.validBytes = bytes;\n        return bytes;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public AbstractIterator<MutableRecordBatch> batchIterator() {\n        return new RecordBatchIterator<>(new ByteBufferLogInputStream(buffer.duplicate(), Integer.MAX_VALUE));\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Validates the header of the first batch and returns batch size.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * This method reads only the batch header (up to and including the record count field) without\n     * deserializing the entire batch. The filtering process handles:\n     * <ul>\n     *   <li>Batch-level retention decisions (DELETE, RETAIN_EMPTY, DELETE_EMPTY)</li>\n     *   <li>Record-level retention decisions via shouldRetainRecord()</li>\n     *   <li>Automatic handling of delete horizons for tombstones and transaction markers</li>\n     *   <li>Decompression and recompression as needed</li>\n     * </ul>\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * <strong>Performance Note:</strong> For small record batches, allocating a large decompression\n     * buffer (e.g., 64 KB for LZ4) can dominate the cost of decompressing and iterating. A buffer\n     * supplier that reuses buffers will have a significant performance impact.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param filter The filter function that determines which records/batches to     * @return A FilterResult with a summary of the output (for metrics) and potentially an overflow buffer\n     * @see RecordFilter for the filtering interface\n     */\n    public FilterResult
