   }\n\n    /**\n     * Note: This method is also used to convert the first timestamp of the batch (which is usually the timestamp of the first record)\n     * to the delete horizon of the tombstones or txn markers which are present in the batch.\n     */\n    private static FilterResult filterTo(Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches, RecordFilter filter,\n                                         ByteBuffer destinationBuffer, BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier) {\n        FilterResult filterResult = new FilterResult(destinationBuffer);\n        ByteBufferOutputStream bufferOutputStream = new ByteBufferOutputStream(destinationBuffer);\n        for (MutableRecordBatch batch : batches) {\n            final BatchRetentionResult batchRetentionResult = filter.checkBatchRetention(batch);\n            final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn = batchRetentionResult.containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n            final BatchRetention batchRetention = batchRetentionResult.batchRetention;\n\n            filterResult.bytesRead += batch.sizeInBytes();\n\n            if (batchRetention == BatchRetention.DELETE)\n                continue;\n\n            final BatchFilterResult iterationResult = filterBatch(batch, decompressionBufferSupplier, filterResult,\n                filter);\n            List<Record> retainedRecords = iterationResult.retainedRecords;\n            boolean containsTombstones = iterationResult.containsTombstones;\n            boolean writeOriginalBatch = iterationResult.writeOriginalBatch;\n            long maxOffset = iterationResult.maxOffset;\n\n            if (!retainedRecords.isEmpty()) {\n                // we check if the delete horizon should be set to a new value\n                // in which case, we need to reset the base timestamp and overwrite the timestamp deltas\n                // if the batch does not contain tombstones, then we don't need to overwrite batch\n                boolean needToSetDeleteHorizon = (containsTombstones || containsMarkerForEmptyTxn) &&\n                    batch.deleteHorizonMs().isEmpty();\n                if (writeOriginalBatch && !needToSetDeleteHorizon) {\n                    batch.writeTo(bufferOutputStream);\n                    filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(batch, retainedRecords.size(), false);\n                } else {\n                    long deleteHorizonMs;\n                    if (needToSetDeleteHorizon)\n                        deleteHorizonMs = filter.currentTime + filter.deleteRetentionMs;\n                    else\n                        deleteHorizonMs = batch.deleteHorizonMs().orElse(RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP);\n                    try (final MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = buildRetainedRecordsInto(batch, retainedRecords,\n                            bufferOutputStream, deleteHorizonMs)) {\n                        MemoryRecords records = builder.build();\n                        int filteredBatchSize = records.sizeInBytes();\n                        MemoryRecordsBuilder.RecordsInfo info = builder.info();\n                        filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(info.maxTimestamp, info.shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp,\n                            maxOffset, retainedRecords.size(), filteredBatchSize);\n                    }\n                }\n            } else if (batchRetention == BatchRetention.RETAIN_EMPTY) {\n                if (batch.magic() < RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2) // should never happen\n                    throw new IllegalStateException(\"Empty batches are only supported for magic v2 and above\");\n\n                bufferOutputStream.ensureRemaining(DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD);\n                DefaultRecordBatch.writeEmptyHeader(bufferOutputStream.buffer(), RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, batch.producerId(),\n                        batch.producerEpoch(), batch.baseSequence(), batch.baseOffset(), batch.lastOffset(),\n                        batch.partitionLeaderEpoch(), batch.timestampType(), batch.maxTimestamp(),\n                        batch.isTransactional(), batch.isControlBatch());\n                filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(batch, 0, true);\n            }\n\n            // If we had to allocate a new buffer to fit the filtered buffer (see KAFKA-5316), return early to\n            // avoid the need for additional allocations.\n            ByteBuffer outputBuffer = bufferOutputStream.buffer();\n            if (outputBuffer != destinationBuffer) {\n                filterResult.outputBuffer = outputBuffer;\n                return filterResult;\n            }\n        }\n\n        return filterResult;\n    }\n\n    private static BatchFilterResult filterBatch(RecordBatch batch,\n                                                 BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier,\n                                                 FilterResult filterResult,\n                                                 RecordFilter filter) {\n        try (final CloseableIterator<Record> iterator = batch.streamingIterator(decompressionBufferSupplier)) {\n            long maxOffset = -1;\n            boolean containsTombstones = false;\n            // Convert records with old record versions\n            boolean writeOriginalBatch = batch.magic() >= RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE;\n            List<Record> retainedRecords = new ArrayList<>();\n            while (iterator.hasNext()) {\n                Record record = iterator.next();\n                filterResult.messagesRead += 1;\n\n                if (filter.shouldRetainRecord(batch, record)) {\n                    if (record.offset() > maxOffset)\n                        maxOffset = record.offset();\n\n                    retainedRecords.add(record);\n\n                    if (!record.hasValue()) {\n                        containsTombstones = true;\n                    }\n                } else {\n                    writeOriginalBatch = false;\n                }\n            }\n            return new BatchFilterResult(retainedRecords, writeOriginalBatch, containsTombstones, maxOffset);\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static class BatchFilterResult {\n        private final List<Record> retainedRecords;\n        private final boolean writeOriginalBatch;\n        private final boolean containsTombstones;\n        private final long maxOffset;\n        private BatchFilterResult(List<Record> retainedRecords,\n                                  final boolean writeOriginalBatch,\n                                  final boolean containsTombstones,\n                                  final long maxOffset) {\n            this.retainedRecords = retainedRecords;\n            this.writeOriginalBatch = writeOriginalBatch;\n            this.containsTombstones = containsTombstones;\n            this.maxOffset = maxOffset;\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static MemoryRecordsBuilder buildRetainedRecordsInto(RecordBatch originalBatch,\n                                                                 List<Record> retainedRecords,\n                                                                 ByteBufferOutputStream bufferOutputStream,\n                                                                 final long deleteHorizonMs) {\n        Compression compression = Compression.of(originalBatch.compressionType()).build();\n        // V0 has no timestamp type or timestamp, so we set the timestamp to CREATE_TIME and timestamp to NO_TIMESTAMP.\n        // Note that this differs from produce up-conversion where the timestamp type topic config is used and the log append\n        // time is generated if the config is LOG_APPEND_TIME. The reason for the different behavior is that there is\n        // no appropriate log append time we can generate at compaction time.\n        TimestampType timestampType = originalBatch.timestampType() == TimestampType.NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE ?\n                TimestampType.CREATE_TIME : originalBatch.timestampType();\n        long logAppendTime = timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME ?\n                originalBatch.maxTimestamp() : RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        long baseOffset = originalBatch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2 ?\n                originalBatch.baseOffset() : retainedRecords.get(0).offset();\n\n        // Convert records with older record versions to the current one\n        MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = new MemoryRecordsBuilder(bufferOutputStream, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE,\n                compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime, originalBatch.producerId(),\n                originalBatch.producerEpoch(), originalBatch.baseSequence(), originalBatch.isTransactional(),\n                originalBatch.isControlBatch(), originalBatch.partitionLeaderEpoch(), bufferOutputStream.limit(), deleteHorizonMs);\n\n        for (Record record : retainedRecords)\n            builder.append(record);\n\n        if (originalBatch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2)\n            // we must preserve the last offset from the initial batch in order to ensure that the\n            // last sequence number from the batch remains even after compaction. Otherwise, the producer\n            // could incorrectly see an out of sequence error.\n            builder.overrideLastOffset(originalBatch.lastOffset());\n\n        return builder;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Get the byte buffer that backs this instance for reading.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * The returned buffer is a duplicate of the internal buffer, so modifications to the returned buffer\n     * will not affect this MemoryRecords instance. However, the underlying byte data is shared.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @return A duplicate view of the backing buffer\n     */\n    public ByteBuffer buffer() {\n        return buffer.duplicate();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new MemoryRecords that represents a slice of this one.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * The returned MemoryRecords shares the underlying buffer with this instance but represents\n     * only the region from position to position+size.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param position The starting position in the buffer\n     * @param size The size of the slice\n     * @return A new MemoryRecords representing the sliced region\n     * @throws IllegalArgumentException if position or size is invalid\n     */\n    public MemoryRecords slice(int position, int size) {\n        if (position < 0)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid position: \" + position + \" in read from \" + this);\n        if (position > buffer.limit())\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Slice from position \" + position + \" exceeds end position of \" + this);\n        if (size < 0)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid size: \" + size + \" in read from \" + this);\n\n        int availableBytes = Math.min(size, buffer.limit() - position);\n        // As of now, clients module support Java11 hence can't use ByteBuffer::slice(position, size) method.\n        // So we need to create a duplicate buffer and set the position and limit. Duplicate buffer\n        // is backed by original bytes hence not the content but only the relative position and limit\n        // are changed in the duplicate buffer. Once the position and limit are set, we can call the\n        // slice method to get the sliced buffer, which is a backed by the original buffer with the\n        // position reset to 0 and limit set to the size of the slice.\n        ByteBuffer slicedBuffer = buffer.duplicate();\n        slicedBuffer.position(position);\n        slicedBuffer.limit(position + availableBytes);\n        // Reset the position to 0 so that the sliced view has a relative position.\n        slicedBuffer = slicedBuffer.slice();\n\n        return readableRecords(slicedBuffer);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches() {\n        return batches;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return \"MemoryRecords(size=\" + sizeInBytes() +\n                \", buffer=\" + buffer +\n                \")\";\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean equals(Object o) {\n        if (this == o)\n            return true;\n        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass())\n            return false;\n\n        MemoryRecords that = (MemoryRecords) o;\n\n        return buffer.equals(that.buffer);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int hashCode() {\n        return buffer.hashCode();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * A filter for selectively retaining or discarding records during log compaction or filtering operations.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * Implementations must define two decision points:\n     * <ul>\n     *   <li>{@link #checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch)} - determines if an entire batch should be deleted/retained/kept-if-empty</li>\n     *   <li>{@link #shouldRetainRecord(RecordBatch, Record)} - determines if an individual record should be retained</li>\n     * </ul>\n     * </p>\n     */\n    public abstract static class RecordFilter {\n        /**\n         * The current time in milliseconds (used for delete horizon calculation).\n         */\n        public final long currentTime;\n        /**\n         * The retention time in milliseconds for delete markers and transaction markers.\n         */\n        public final long deleteRetentionMs;\n\n        /**\n         * Construct a RecordFilter.\n         *\n         * @param currentTime The current time in milliseconds\n         * @param deleteRetentionMs The retention time in milliseconds for delete markers\n         */\n        public RecordFilter(final long currentTime, final long deleteRetentionMs) {\n            this.currentTime = currentTime;\n            this.deleteRetentionMs = deleteRetentionMs;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Result of {@link #checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch)}.\n         */\n        public static class BatchRetentionResult {\n            /**\n             * The batch retention decision.\n             */\n            public final BatchRetention batchRetention;\n            /**\n             * Whether this batch contains a marker for an empty transaction.\n             */\n            public final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n\n            /**\n             * Construct a BatchRetentionResult.\n             *\n             * @param batchRetention The batch retention decision\n             * @param containsMarkerForEmptyTxn Whether an empty transaction marker is present\n             */\n            public BatchRetentionResult(final BatchRetention batchRetention,\n                                        final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn) {\n                this.batchRetention = batchRetention;\n                this.containsMarkerForEmptyTxn = containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n            }\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Batch retention decision enumeration.\n         */\n        public enum BatchRetention {\n            /**\n             * Delete the batch without inspecting records.\n             */\n            DELETE,\n            /**\n             * Retain the batch even if it becomes empty after record filtering.\n             */\n            RETAIN_EMPTY,\n            /**\n             * Delete the batch if it becomes empty after record filtering.\n             */\n            DELETE_EMPTY\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Check whether the full batch can be discarded (i.e. whether we even need to\n         * check the records individually).\n         *\n         * <p>\n         * This method is called before individual record filtering. Returning {@link BatchRetention#DELETE}\n         * will skip record-level filtering and immediately discard the batch.\n         * </p>\n         *\n         * @param batch The batch to evaluate\n         * @return A BatchRetentionResult indicating the retention decision\n         */\n        protected abstract BatchRetentionResult checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch batch);\n\n        /**\n         * Check whether a record should be retained in the log.\n         *\n         * <p>\n         * Note that {@link #checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch)} is used prior to checking individual record retention.\n         * Only records from batches which were not explicitly discarded with {@link BatchRetention#DELETE} will be considered.\n         * </p>\n         *\n         * @param recordBatch The batch containing the record\n         * @param record The record to evaluate\n         * @return true if the record should be retained, false otherwise\n         */\n        protected abstract boolean shouldRetainRecord(RecordBatch recordBatch, Record record);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Result of filtering records via {@link #filterTo(RecordFilter, ByteBuffer, BufferSupplier)}.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * Contains statistics about the filtering operation and the output buffer containing filtered records.\n     * </p>\n     */\n    public static class FilterResult {\n        /**\n         * The output buffer containing filtered records. May differ from the input buffer if reallocation was necessary.\n         */\n        private ByteBuffer outputBuffer;\n        /**\n         * Total number of input records examined (including filtered-out records).\n         */\n        private int messagesRead = 0;\n        /**\n         * Total number of input bytes examined (including filtered-out batches).\n         */\n        private int bytesRead = 0;\n        /**\n         * Number of records retained in the output.\n         */\n        private int messagesRetained = 0;\n        /**\n         * Number of bytes retained in the output.\n         */\n        private int bytesRetained = 0;\n        /**\n         * The maximum offset among retained records.\n         */\n        private long maxOffset = -1L;\n        /**\n         * The maximum timestamp among retained records.\n         */\n        private long maxTimestamp = RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        /**\n         * The offset of the record with the maximum timestamp.\n         */\n        private long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp = -1L;\n\n        /**\n         * Construct a FilterResult with an initial output buffer.\n         *\n         * @param outputBuffer The output buffer\n         */\n        private FilterResult(ByteBuffer outputBuffer) {\n            this.outputBuffer = outputBuffer;\n        }\n\n        private void updateRetainedBatchMetadata(MutableRecordBatch retainedBatch, int numMessagesInBatch, boolean headerOnly) {\n            int bytesRetained = headerOnly ? DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD : retainedBatch.sizeInBytes();\n            updateRetainedBatchMetadata(retainedBatch.maxTimestamp(), retainedBatch.lastOffset(),\n                    retainedBatch.lastOffset(), numMessagesInBatch, bytesRetained);\n        }\n\n        private void updateRetainedBatchMetadata(long maxTimestamp, long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, long maxOffset,\n                                                 int messagesRetained, int bytesRetained) {\n            validateBatchMetadata(maxTimestamp, shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, maxOffset);\n            if (maxTimestamp > this.maxTimestamp) {\n                this.maxTimestamp = maxTimestamp;\n                this.shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp = shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp;\n            }\n            this.maxOffset = Math.max(maxOffset, this.maxOffset);\n            this.messagesRetained += messagesRetained;\n            this.bytesRetained += bytesRetained;\n        }\n\n        private void validateBatchMetadata(long maxTimestamp, long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, long maxOffset) {\n            if (maxTimestamp != RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP && shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp < 0)\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"shallowOffset undefined for maximum timestamp \" + maxTimestamp);\n            if (maxOffset < 0)\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"maxOffset undefined\");\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the output buffer containing filtered records.\n         *\n         * @return The output buffer\n         */\n        public ByteBuffer outputBuffer() {\n            return outputBuffer;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the total number of messages examined during filtering.\n         *\n         * @return The number of messages read\n         */\n        public int messagesRead() {\n            return messagesRead;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the total number of bytes examined during filtering.\n         *\n         * @return The number of bytes read\n         */\n        public int bytesRead() {\n            return bytesRead;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the number of messages retained in the filtered output.\n         *\n         * @return The number of messages retained\n         */\n        public int messagesRetained() {\n            return messagesRetained;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the number of bytes retained in the filtered output.\n         *\n         * @return The number of bytes retained\n         */\n        public int bytesRetained() {\n            return bytesRetained;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the maximum offset among retained records.\n         *\n         * @return The max offset, or -1 if no records were retained\n         */\n        public long maxOffset() {\n            return maxOffset;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the maximum timestamp among retained records.\n         *\n         * @return The max timestamp, or NO_TIMESTAMP if no records were retained\n         */\n        public long maxTimestamp() {\n            return maxTimestamp;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the offset of the record with the maximum timestamp.\n         *\n         * @return The offset of max timestamp, or -1 if no records were retained\n         */\n        public long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp() {\n            return shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new MemoryRecords backed by the provided buffer.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * The buffer should contain valid record batch data. Multiple MemoryRecords can be created\n     * from the same buffer, and they will share the underlying byte data.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to wrap\n     * @return A new MemoryRecords instance\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords readableRecords(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        return new MemoryRecords(buffer);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new MemoryRecordsBuilder for building record batches.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * Uses default values for producer ID, epoch, sequence, and leader epoch.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to write to\n     * @param compression The compression type\n     * @param timestampType The timestamp type\n     * @param baseOffset The base offset for the batch\n     * @return A new MemoryRecordsBuilder\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset) {\n        return builder(buffer, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression, timestampType, baseOffset);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new MemoryRecordsBuilder with a maximum size constraint.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to write to\n     * @param compression The compression type\n     * @param timestampType The timestamp type\n     * @param baseOffset The base offset for the batch\n     * @param maxSize The maximum size of the batch\n     * @return A new MemoryRecordsBuilder\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               int maxSize) {\n        long logAppendTime = RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME)\n            logAppendTime = System.currentTimeMillis();\n\n        return new MemoryRecordsBuilder(buffer, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression, timestampType, baseOffset,\n            logAppendTime, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH, RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE,\n            false, false, RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH, maxSize);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new MemoryRecordsBuilder with a specified magic version and log append time.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to write to\n     * @param magic The magic version\n     * @param compression The compression type\n     * @param timestampType The timestamp type\n     * @param baseOffset The base offset for the batch\n     * @param logAppendTime The log append time (for LOG_APPEND_TIME batches)\n     * @return A new MemoryRecordsBuilder\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               byte magic,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               long logAppendTime) {\n        return builder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH, RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE, false,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new MemoryRecordsBuilder with a specified magic version.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to write to\n     * @param magic The magic version\n     * @param compression The compression type\n     * @param timestampType The timestamp type\n     * @param baseOffset The base offset for the batch\n     * @return A new MemoryRecordsBuilder\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               byte magic,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset) {\n        long logAppendTime = RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME)\n            logAppendTime = System.currentTimeMillis();\n        return builder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH, RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE, false,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new MemoryRecordsBuilder with partition leader epoch.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to write to\n     * @param magic The magic version\n     * @param compression The compression type\n     * @param timestampType The timestamp type\n     * @param baseOffset The base offset for the batch\n     * @param logAppendTime The log append time\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The partition leader epoch\n     * @return A new MemoryRecordsBuilder\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               byte magic,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               long logAppendTime,\n                                               int partitionLeaderEpoch) {\n        return builder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH, RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE, false, partitionLeaderEpoch);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new MemoryRecordsBuilder for idempotent records.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to write to\n     * @param compression The compression type\n     * @param baseOffset The base offset for the batch\n     * @param producerId The producer ID\n     * @param producerEpoch The producer epoch\n     * @param baseSequence The base sequence number\n     * @param isTransactional Whether the records are transactional\n     * @return A new                  long baseOffset,\n                                               long producerId,\n                                               short producerEpoch,\n                                               int baseSequence,\n                                               boolean isTransactional) {\n        return builder(buffer, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression,  }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new MemoryRecordsBuilder with producer information.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to write to\n     * @param magic The magic version\n     * @param MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               byte magic,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               long logAppendTime,\n                                               long producerId,\n                                               short producerEpoch,\n                                               int baseSequence) {\n        return builder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime,\n                producerId, producerEpoch, baseSequence, false, RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new MemoryRecordsBuilder with full control over all parameters.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to write to\n     * @param magic The magic version\n     * @param   * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The partition leader epoch\n     * @return A new MemoryRecordsBuilder\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               byte magic,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               long logAppendTime,\n                                               long producerId,\n                                               short producerEpoch,\n                                               int baseSequence,\n                                               boolean isTransactional,\n                                               int partitionLeaderEpoch) {\n        return builder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset,\n                logAppendTime, producerId, producerEpoch, baseSequence, isTransactional, false, partitionLeaderEpoch);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new MemoryRecordsBuilder with control batch support.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The number\n     * @param isTransactional Whether the records are transactional\n     * @param isControlBatch Whether this is a control batch\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The partition leader                                 Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               long logAppendTime,\n                                               long producerId,\n                                               short  boolean isControlBatch,\n                                               int partitionLeaderEpoch) {\n        return new MemoryRecordsBuilder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset,\n                logAppendTime, producerId, producerEpoch, baseSequence, isTransactional, isControlBatch, partitionLeaderEpoch,\n                buffer.remaining());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create MemoryRecords from simple records.\n     *\n     * @param compression The compression type\n     * @param records The records to include\n     * @return A new MemoryRecords containing the records\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withRecords(Compression compression, SimpleRecord... records) {\n        return withRecords(RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression, records);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create MemoryRecords with partition leader epoch.\n     *\n     * @param compression The compression type\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The partition leader epoch\n     * @param records The records to include\n     * @return A new MemoryRecords\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withRecords(Compression compression, int partitionLeaderEpoch, SimpleRecord... records) {\n        return withRecords(RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, 0L, compression, TimestampType.CREATE_TIME,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH, RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE,\n                partitionLeaderEpoch, false, records);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create MemoryRecords with a specific magic version.\n     *\n     * @param magic The magic version\n     * @param compression The compression type\n     * @param records The records to include\n     * @return A new MemoryRecords\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withRecords(byte magic, Compression compression, SimpleRecord... records) {\n        return withRecords(magic, 0L, compression, TimestampType.CREATE_TIME, records);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create MemoryRecords with a specific initial offset.\n     *\n     * @param initialOffset The initial offset\n     * @param compression The compression type\n     * @param records The records to include\n     * @return A new MemoryRecords\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withRecords(long initialOffset, Compression compression, SimpleRecord... records) {\n        return withRecords(RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, initialOffset, compression, TimestampType.CREATE_TIME,\n                records);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create MemoryRecords with magic version and initial offset.\n     *\n     * @param magic The This is used for reading and\n * in-place modification of existing record batches. To create new record batches, use\n * {@link MemoryRecordsBuilder} or the {@link #builder(ByteBuffer, Compression, TimestampType, long)} static factory methods.\n *\n * <p>\n * <strong>Thread Safety:</strong> This class is NOT thread-safe. The underlying ByteBuffer may be modified\n * by filtering operations and other mutations. Callers must ensure external synchronization if shared across threads.\n * </p>\n *\n * <p>\n * <strong>Memory Model:</strong> MemoryRecords maintains a reference to a ByteBuffer but does not copy it.\n * Multiple MemoryRecords instances can be created from the same buffer (via {@link #slice(int, int)}),\n * and they will share the underlying data.\n * </p>\n *\n * @see DefaultRecordBatch for the batch format implementation\n * @see MemoryRecordsBuilder for building new MemoryRecords\n * @see Records for the parent interface\n */\npublic class MemoryRecords extends AbstractRecords {\n    /**\n     * An empty MemoryRecords instance backed by an empty buffer.\n     */\n    public static final MemoryRecords EMPTY = MemoryRecords.readableRecords(ByteBuffer.allocate(0));\n\n    private final ByteBuffer buffer;\n\n    private final Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches = this::batchIterator;\n\n    private int validBytes = -1;\n\n    /**\n     * Construct a MemoryRecords from a ByteBuffer.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * The buffer should contain one or more record batches. The buffer's position and limit\n     * define the region of valid data. The buffer is not copied; a reference to it is maintained.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param buffer The ByteBuffer containing record batch data. Must not be null.\n     * @throws NullPointerException if buffer is null\n     */\n    private MemoryRecords(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        Objects.requireNonNull(buffer, \"buffer should not be null\");\n        this.buffer = buffer;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int sizeInBytes() {\n        return buffer.limit();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int writeTo(TransferableChannel channel, int position, int length) throws IOException {\n        if (((long) position) + length > buffer.limit())\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"position+length should not be greater than buffer.limit(), position: \"\n                    + position + \", length: \" + length + \", buffer.limit(): \" + buffer.limit());\n\n        return Utils.tryWriteTo(channel, position, length, buffer);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Write all records to the given channel (including partial records).\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * This method writes the entire buffer contents to the channel, including any partial batches\n     * at the end. It resets the buffer's position after writing completes.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param channel The channel to write to\n     * @return The number of bytes written\n     * @throws IOException For any IO errors writing to the channel\n     */\n    public int writeFullyTo(GatheringByteChannel channel) throws IOException {\n        buffer.mark();\n        int written = 0;\n        while (written < sizeInBytes())\n            written += channel.write(buffer);\n        buffer.reset();\n        return written;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * The total number of bytes in this message set not including any partial, trailing messages. This\n     * may be smaller than what is returned by {@link #sizeInBytes()} if the buffer contains incomplete batches.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * <strong>Performance Note:</strong> This method caches the result on first call. Subsequent calls return\n     * the cached value unless the MemoryRecords is modified.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @return The number of valid bytes (complete batches only)\n     */\n    public int validBytes() {\n        if (validBytes >= 0)\n            return validBytes;\n\n        int bytes = 0;\n        for (RecordBatch batch : batches())\n            bytes += batch.sizeInBytes();\n\n        this.validBytes = bytes;\n        return bytes;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public AbstractIterator<MutableRecordBatch> batchIterator() {\n        return new RecordBatchIterator<>(new ByteBufferLogInputStream(buffer.duplicate(), Integer.MAX_VALUE));\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Validates the header of the first batch and returns batch size.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * This method reads only the batch header (up to and including the record count field) without\n     * deserializing the entire batch. It is useful for checking if a complete batch is present\n     * without reading all its records.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @return first batch size including LOG_OVERHEAD if buffer contains a complete header,\n     *         null if the buffer doesn't contain enough bytes for a complete header\n     * @throws CorruptRecordException if record size or magic is invalid\n     */\n    public Integer firstBatchSize() {\n        if (buffer.remaining() < HEADER_SIZE_UP_TO_MAGIC)\n            return null;\n        return new ByteBufferLogInputStream(buffer, Integer.MAX_VALUE).nextBatchSize();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Filter the records into the provided ByteBuffer.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * This method applies the provided filter to each batch and record, producing a new ByteBuffer\n     * containing only the records that pass the filter. The filtering process handles:\n     * <ul>\n     *   <li>Batch-level retention decisions (DELETE, RETAIN_EMPTY, DELETE_EMPTY)</li>\n     *   <li>Record-level retention decisions via shouldRetainRecord()</li>\n     *   <li>Automatic handling of delete horizons for tombstones and transaction markers</li>\n     *   <li>Decompression and recompression as needed</li>\n     * </ul>\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * <strong>Performance Note:</strong> For small record batches, allocating a large decompression\n     * buffer (e.g., 64 KB for LZ4) can dominate the cost of decompressing and iterating. A buffer\n     * supplier that reuses buffers will have a significant performance impact.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param filter The filter function that determines which records/batches to retain\n     * @param destinationBuffer The byte buffer to write the filtered records to\n     * @param decompressionBufferSupplier The supplier of ByteBuffer(s) used for decompression if supported.\n     * @return A FilterResult with a summary of the output (for metrics) and potentially an overflow buffer\n     * @see RecordFilter for the filtering interface\n     */\n    public FilterResult filterTo(RecordFilter filter, ByteBuffer destinationBuffer, BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier) {\n        return filterTo(batches(), filter, destinationBuffer, decompressionBufferSupplier);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Note: This method is also used to convert the first timestamp of the batch (which is usually the timestamp of the first record)\n     * to the delete horizon of the tombstones or txn markers which are present in the batch.\n     */\n    private static FilterResult filterTo(Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches, RecordFilter filter,\n                                         ByteBuffer destinationBuffer, BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier) {\n        FilterResult filterResult = new FilterResult(destinationBuffer);\n        ByteBufferOutputStream bufferOutputStream = new ByteBufferOutputStream(destinationBuffer);\n        for (MutableRecordBatch batch : batches) {\n            final BatchRetentionResult batchRetentionResult = filter.checkBatchRetention(batch);\n            final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn = batchRetentionResult.containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n            final BatchRetention batchRetention = batchRetentionResult.batchRetention;\n\n            filterResult.bytesRead += batch.sizeInBytes();\n\n            if (batchRetention == BatchRetention.DELETE)\n                continue;\n\n            final BatchFilterResult iterationResult = filterBatch(batch, decompressionBufferSupplier, filterResult,\n                filter);\n            List<Record> retainedRecords = iterationResult.retainedRecords;\n            boolean containsTombstones = iterationResult.containsTombstones;\n            boolean writeOriginalBatch = iterationResult.writeOriginalBatch;\n            long maxOffset = iterationResult.maxOffset;\n\n            if (!retainedRecords.isEmpty()) {\n                // we check if the delete horizon should be set to a new value\n                // in which case, we need to reset the base timestamp and overwrite the timestamp deltas\n                // if the batch does not contain tombstones, then we don't need to overwrite batch\n                boolean needToSetDeleteHorizon = (containsTombstones || containsMarkerForEmptyTxn) &&\n                    batch.deleteHorizonMs().isEmpty();\n                if (writeOriginalBatch && !needToSetDeleteHorizon) {\n                    batch.writeTo(bufferOutputStream);\n                    filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(batch, retainedRecords.size(), false);\n                } else {\n                    long deleteHorizonMs;\n                    if (needToSetDeleteHorizon)\n                        deleteHorizonMs = filter.currentTime + filter.deleteRetentionMs;\n                    else\n                        deleteHorizonMs = batch.deleteHorizonMs().orElse(RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP);\n                    try (final MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = buildRetainedRecordsInto(batch, retainedRecords,\n                            bufferOutputStream, deleteHorizonMs)) {\n                        MemoryRecords records = builder.build();\n                        int filteredBatchSize = records.sizeInBytes();\n                        MemoryRecordsBuilder.RecordsInfo info = builder.info();\n                        filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(info.maxTimestamp, info.shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp,\n                            maxOffset, retainedRecords.size(), filteredBatchSize);\n                    }\n                }\n            } else if (batchRetention == BatchRetention.RETAIN_EMPTY) {\n                if (batch.magic() < RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2) // should never happen\n                    throw new IllegalStateException(\"Empty batches are only supported for magic v2 and above\");\n\n                bufferOutputStream.ensureRemaining(DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD);\n                DefaultRecordBatch.writeEmptyHeader(bufferOutputStream.buffer(), RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, batch.producerId(),\n                        batch.producerEpoch(), batch.baseSequence(), batch.baseOffset(), batch.lastOffset(),\n                        batch.partitionLeaderEpoch(), batch.timestampType(), batch.maxTimestamp(),\n                        batch.isTransactional(), batch.isControlBatch());\n                filterResult.updateRetainedBatchMetadata(batch, 0, true);\n            }\n\n            // If we had to allocate a new buffer to fit the filtered buffer (see KAFKA-5316), return early to\n            // avoid the need for additional allocations.\n            ByteBuffer outputBuffer = bufferOutputStream.buffer();\n            if (outputBuffer != destinationBuffer) {\n                filterResult.outputBuffer = outputBuffer;\n                return filterResult;\n            }\n        }\n\n        return filterResult;\n    }\n\n    private static BatchFilterResult filterBatch(RecordBatch batch,\n                                                 BufferSupplier decompressionBufferSupplier,\n                                                 FilterResult filterResult,\n                                                 RecordFilter filter) {\n        try (final CloseableIterator<Record> iterator = batch.streamingIterator(decompressionBufferSupplier)) {\n            long maxOffset = -1;\n            boolean containsTombstones = false;\n            // Convert records with old record versions\n            boolean writeOriginalBatch = batch.magic() >= RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE;\n            List<Record> retainedRecords = new ArrayList<>();\n            while (iterator.hasNext()) {\n                Record record = iterator.next();\n                filterResult.messagesRead += 1;\n\n                if (filter.shouldRetainRecord(batch, record)) {\n                    if (record.offset() > maxOffset)\n                        maxOffset = record.offset();\n\n                    retainedRecords.add(record);\n\n                    if (!record.hasValue()) {\n                        containsTombstones = true;\n                    }\n                } else {\n                    writeOriginalBatch = false;\n                }\n            }\n            return new BatchFilterResult(retainedRecords, writeOriginalBatch, containsTombstones, maxOffset);\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static class BatchFilterResult {\n        private final List<Record> retainedRecords;\n        private final boolean writeOriginalBatch;\n        private final boolean containsTombstones;\n        private final long maxOffset;\n        private BatchFilterResult(List<Record> retainedRecords,\n                                  final boolean writeOriginalBatch,\n                                  final boolean containsTombstones,\n                                  final long maxOffset) {\n            this.retainedRecords = retainedRecords;\n            this.writeOriginalBatch = writeOriginalBatch;\n            this.containsTombstones = containsTombstones;\n            this.maxOffset = maxOffset;\n        }\n    }\n\n    private static MemoryRecordsBuilder buildRetainedRecordsInto(RecordBatch originalBatch,\n                                                                 List<Record> retainedRecords,\n                                                                 ByteBufferOutputStream bufferOutputStream,\n                                                                 final long deleteHorizonMs) {\n        Compression compression = Compression.of(originalBatch.compressionType()).build();\n        // V0 has no timestamp type or timestamp, so we set the timestamp to CREATE_TIME and timestamp to NO_TIMESTAMP.\n        // Note that this differs from produce up-conversion where the timestamp type topic config is used and the log append\n        // time is generated if the config is LOG_APPEND_TIME. The reason for the different behavior is that there is\n        // no appropriate log append time we can generate at compaction time.\n        TimestampType timestampType = originalBatch.timestampType() == TimestampType.NO_TIMESTAMP_TYPE ?\n                TimestampType.CREATE_TIME : originalBatch.timestampType();\n        long logAppendTime = timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME ?\n                originalBatch.maxTimestamp() : RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        long baseOffset = originalBatch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2 ?\n                originalBatch.baseOffset() : retainedRecords.get(0).offset();\n\n        // Convert records with older record versions to the current one\n        MemoryRecordsBuilder builder = new MemoryRecordsBuilder(bufferOutputStream, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE,\n                compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime, originalBatch.producerId(),\n                originalBatch.producerEpoch(), originalBatch.baseSequence(), originalBatch.isTransactional(),\n                originalBatch.isControlBatch(), originalBatch.partitionLeaderEpoch(), bufferOutputStream.limit(), deleteHorizonMs);\n\n        for (Record record : retainedRecords)\n            builder.append(record);\n\n        if (originalBatch.magic() >= RecordBatch.MAGIC_VALUE_V2)\n            // we must preserve the last offset from the initial batch in order to ensure that the\n            // last sequence number from the batch remains even after compaction. Otherwise, the producer\n            // could incorrectly see an out of sequence error.\n            builder.overrideLastOffset(originalBatch.lastOffset());\n\n        return builder;\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Get the byte buffer that backs this instance for reading.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * The returned buffer is a duplicate of the internal buffer, so modifications to the returned buffer\n     * will not affect this MemoryRecords instance. However, the underlying byte data is shared.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @return A duplicate view of the backing buffer\n     */\n    public ByteBuffer buffer() {\n        return buffer.duplicate();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new MemoryRecords that represents a slice of this one.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * The returned MemoryRecords shares the underlying buffer with this instance but represents\n     * only the region from position to position+size.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param position The starting position in the buffer\n     * @param size The size of the slice\n     * @return A new MemoryRecords representing the sliced region\n     * @throws IllegalArgumentException if position or size is invalid\n     */\n    public MemoryRecords slice(int position, int size) {\n        if (position < 0)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid position: \" + position + \" in read from \" + this);\n        if (position > buffer.limit())\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Slice from position \" + position + \" exceeds end position of \" + this);\n        if (size < 0)\n            throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"Invalid size: \" + size + \" in read from \" + this);\n\n        int availableBytes = Math.min(size, buffer.limit() - position);\n        // As of now, clients module support Java11 hence can't use ByteBuffer::slice(position, size) method.\n        // So we need to create a duplicate buffer and set the position and limit. Duplicate buffer\n        // is backed by original bytes hence not the content but only the relative position and limit\n        // are changed in the duplicate buffer. Once the position and limit are set, we can call the\n        // slice method to get the sliced buffer, which is a backed by the original buffer with the\n        // position reset to 0 and limit set to the size of the slice.\n        ByteBuffer slicedBuffer = buffer.duplicate();\n        slicedBuffer.position(position);\n        slicedBuffer.limit(position + availableBytes);\n        // Reset the position to 0 so that the sliced view has a relative position.\n        slicedBuffer = slicedBuffer.slice();\n\n        return readableRecords(slicedBuffer);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Iterable<MutableRecordBatch> batches() {\n        return batches;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public String toString() {\n        return \"MemoryRecords(size=\" + sizeInBytes() +\n                \", buffer=\" + buffer +\n                \")\";\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public boolean equals(Object o) {\n        if (this == o)\n            return true;\n        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass())\n            return false;\n\n        MemoryRecords that = (MemoryRecords) o;\n\n        return buffer.equals(that.buffer);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public int hashCode() {\n        return buffer.hashCode();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * A filter for selectively retaining or discarding records during log compaction or filtering operations.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * Implementations must define two decision points:\n     * <ul>\n     *   <li>{@link #checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch)} - determines if an entire batch should be deleted/retained/kept-if-empty</li>\n     *   <li>{@link #shouldRetainRecord(RecordBatch, Record)} - determines if an individual record should be retained</li>\n     * </ul>\n     * </p>\n     */\n    public abstract static class RecordFilter {\n        /**\n         * The current time in milliseconds (used for delete horizon calculation).\n         */\n        public final long currentTime;\n        /**\n         * The retention time in milliseconds for delete markers and transaction markers.\n         */\n        public final long deleteRetentionMs;\n\n        /**\n         * Construct a RecordFilter.\n         *\n         * @param currentTime The current time in milliseconds\n         * @param deleteRetentionMs The retention time in milliseconds for delete markers\n         */\n        public RecordFilter(final long currentTime, final long deleteRetentionMs) {\n            this.currentTime = currentTime;\n            this.deleteRetentionMs = deleteRetentionMs;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Result of {@link #checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch)}.\n         */\n        public static class BatchRetentionResult {\n            /**\n             * The batch retention decision.\n             */\n            public final BatchRetention batchRetention;\n            /**\n             * Whether this batch contains a marker for an empty transaction.\n             */\n            public final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n\n            /**\n             * Construct a BatchRetentionResult.\n             *\n             * @param batchRetention The batch retention decision\n             * @param containsMarkerForEmptyTxn Whether an empty transaction marker is present\n             */\n            public BatchRetentionResult(final BatchRetention batchRetention,\n                                        final boolean containsMarkerForEmptyTxn) {\n                this.batchRetention = batchRetention;\n                this.containsMarkerForEmptyTxn = containsMarkerForEmptyTxn;\n            }\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Batch retention decision enumeration.\n         */\n        public enum BatchRetention {\n            /**\n             * Delete the batch without inspecting records.\n             */\n            DELETE,\n            /**\n             * Retain the batch even if it becomes empty after record filtering.\n             */\n            RETAIN_EMPTY,\n            /**\n             * Delete the batch if it becomes empty after record filtering.\n             */\n            DELETE_EMPTY\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Check whether the full batch can be discarded (i.e. whether we even need to\n         * check the records individually).\n         *\n         * <p>\n         * This method is called before individual record filtering. Returning {@link BatchRetention#DELETE}\n         * will skip record-level filtering and immediately discard the batch.\n         * </p>\n         *\n         * @param batch The batch to evaluate\n         * @return A BatchRetentionResult indicating the retention decision\n         */\n        protected abstract BatchRetentionResult checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch batch);\n\n        /**\n         * Check whether a record should be retained in the log.\n         *\n         * <p>\n         * Note that {@link #checkBatchRetention(RecordBatch)} is used prior to checking individual record retention.\n         * Only records from batches which were not explicitly discarded with {@link BatchRetention#DELETE} will be considered.\n         * </p>\n         *\n         * @param recordBatch The batch containing the record\n         * @param record The record to evaluate\n         * @return true if the record should be retained, false otherwise\n         */\n        protected abstract boolean shouldRetainRecord(RecordBatch recordBatch, Record record);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Result of filtering records via {@link #filterTo(RecordFilter, ByteBuffer, BufferSupplier)}.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * Contains statistics about the filtering operation and the output buffer containing filtered records.\n     * </p>\n     */\n    public static class FilterResult {\n        /**\n         * The output buffer containing filtered records. May differ from the input buffer if reallocation was necessary.\n         */\n        private ByteBuffer outputBuffer;\n        /**\n         * Total number of input records examined (including filtered-out records).\n         */\n        private int messagesRead = 0;\n        /**\n         * Total number of input bytes examined (including filtered-out batches).\n         */\n        private int bytesRead = 0;\n        /**\n         * Number of records retained in the output.\n         */\n        private int messagesRetained = 0;\n        /**\n         * Number of bytes retained in the output.\n         */\n        private int bytesRetained = 0;\n        /**\n         * The maximum offset among retained records.\n         */\n        private long maxOffset = -1L;\n        /**\n         * The maximum timestamp among retained records.\n         */\n        private long maxTimestamp = RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        /**\n         * The offset of the record with the maximum timestamp.\n         */\n        private long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp = -1L;\n\n        /**\n         * Construct a FilterResult with an initial output buffer.\n         *\n         * @param outputBuffer The output buffer\n         */\n        private FilterResult(ByteBuffer outputBuffer) {\n            this.outputBuffer = outputBuffer;\n        }\n\n        private void updateRetainedBatchMetadata(MutableRecordBatch retainedBatch, int numMessagesInBatch, boolean headerOnly) {\n            int bytesRetained = headerOnly ? DefaultRecordBatch.RECORD_BATCH_OVERHEAD : retainedBatch.sizeInBytes();\n            updateRetainedBatchMetadata(retainedBatch.maxTimestamp(), retainedBatch.lastOffset(),\n                    retainedBatch.lastOffset(), numMessagesInBatch, bytesRetained);\n        }\n\n        private void updateRetainedBatchMetadata(long maxTimestamp, long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, long maxOffset,\n                                                 int messagesRetained, int bytesRetained) {\n            validateBatchMetadata(maxTimestamp, shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, maxOffset);\n            if (maxTimestamp > this.maxTimestamp) {\n                this.maxTimestamp = maxTimestamp;\n                this.shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp = shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp;\n            }\n            this.maxOffset = Math.max(maxOffset, this.maxOffset);\n            this.messagesRetained += messagesRetained;\n            this.bytesRetained += bytesRetained;\n        }\n\n        private void validateBatchMetadata(long maxTimestamp, long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp, long maxOffset) {\n            if (maxTimestamp != RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP && shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp < 0)\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"shallowOffset undefined for maximum timestamp \" + maxTimestamp);\n            if (maxOffset < 0)\n                throw new IllegalArgumentException(\"maxOffset undefined\");\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the output buffer containing filtered records.\n         *\n         * @return The output buffer\n         */\n        public ByteBuffer outputBuffer() {\n            return outputBuffer;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the total number of messages examined during filtering.\n         *\n         * @return The number of messages read\n         */\n        public int messagesRead() {\n            return messagesRead;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the total number of bytes examined during filtering.\n         *\n         * @return The number of bytes read\n         */\n        public int bytesRead() {\n            return bytesRead;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the number of messages retained in the filtered output.\n         *\n         * @return The number of messages retained\n         */\n        public int messagesRetained() {\n            return messagesRetained;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the number of bytes retained in the filtered output.\n         *\n         * @return The number of bytes retained\n         */\n        public int bytesRetained() {\n            return bytesRetained;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the maximum offset among retained records.\n         *\n         * @return The max offset, or -1 if no records were retained\n         */\n        public long maxOffset() {\n            return maxOffset;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the maximum timestamp among retained records.\n         *\n         * @return The max timestamp, or NO_TIMESTAMP if no records were retained\n         */\n        public long maxTimestamp() {\n            return maxTimestamp;\n        }\n\n        /**\n         * Get the offset of the record with the maximum timestamp.\n         *\n         * @return The offset of max timestamp, or -1 if no records were retained\n         */\n        public long shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp() {\n            return shallowOffsetOfMaxTimestamp;\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new MemoryRecords backed by the provided buffer.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * The buffer should contain valid record batch data. Multiple MemoryRecords can be created\n     * from the same buffer, and they will share the underlying byte data.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to wrap\n     * @return A new MemoryRecords instance\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords readableRecords(ByteBuffer buffer) {\n        return new MemoryRecords(buffer);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new MemoryRecordsBuilder for building record batches.\n     *\n     * <p>\n     * Uses default values for producer ID, epoch, sequence, and leader epoch.\n     * </p>\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to write to\n     * @param compression The compression type\n     * @param timestampType The timestamp type\n     * @param baseOffset The base offset for the batch\n     * @return A new MemoryRecordsBuilder\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset) {\n        return builder(buffer, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression, timestampType, baseOffset);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new MemoryRecordsBuilder with a maximum size constraint.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to write to\n     * @param compression The compression type\n     * @param timestampType The timestamp type\n     * @param baseOffset The base offset for the batch\n     * @param maxSize The maximum size of the batch\n     * @return A new MemoryRecordsBuilder\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               int maxSize) {\n        long logAppendTime = RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME)\n            logAppendTime = System.currentTimeMillis();\n\n        return new MemoryRecordsBuilder(buffer, RecordBatch.CURRENT_MAGIC_VALUE, compression, timestampType, baseOffset,\n            logAppendTime, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH, RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE,\n            false, false, RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH, maxSize);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new MemoryRecordsBuilder with a specified magic version and log append time.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to write to\n     * @param magic The magic version\n     * @param compression The compression type\n     * @param timestampType The timestamp type\n     * @param baseOffset The base offset for the batch\n     * @param logAppendTime The log append time (for LOG_APPEND_TIME batches)\n     * @return A new MemoryRecordsBuilder\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               byte magic,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               long logAppendTime) {\n        return builder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH, RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE, false,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new MemoryRecordsBuilder with a specified magic version.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to write to\n     * @param magic The magic version\n     * @param compression The compression type\n     * @param timestampType The timestamp type\n     * @param baseOffset The base offset for the batch\n     * @return A new MemoryRecordsBuilder\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecordsBuilder builder(ByteBuffer buffer,\n                                               byte magic,\n                                               Compression compression,\n                                               TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset) {\n        long logAppendTime = RecordBatch.NO_TIMESTAMP;\n        if (timestampType == TimestampType.LOG_APPEND_TIME)\n            logAppendTime = RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE, false,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new MemoryRecordsBuilder with partition leader epoch.\n     *\n     * @param                                    TimestampType timestampType,\n                                               long baseOffset,\n                                               long logAppendTime,\n                                               int partitionLeaderEpoch) {\n        return builder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime,\n                RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_ID, RecordBatch.NO_PRODUCER_EPOCH, RecordBatch.NO_SEQUENCE, false, partitionLeaderEpoch);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new MemoryRecordsBuilder for idempotent records.\n  }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new MemoryRecordsBuilder with producer information.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to write to\n     * @param magic The magic version\n     * @param return builder(buffer, magic, compression, timestampType, baseOffset, logAppendTime,\n                producerId, producerEpoch, baseSequence, false, RecordBatch.NO_PARTITION_LEADER_EPOCH);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create a new MemoryRecordsBuilder with full control over all parameters.\n     *\n     * @param buffer The buffer to write to\n     * @param magic The magic version\n     * @param /**\n     * Create MemoryRecords with partition leader epoch.\n     *\n     * @param compression The compression type\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The partition leader epoch\n     * @param records);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Create idempotent MemoryRecords with magic version.\n     *\n     * @param magic The magic version\n     * @param initialOffset The initial offset\n     * @param compression The compression type\n     * @param producerId The producer ID\n     * @param producerEpoch The producer epoch\n     * @param baseSequence The base sequence number\n     * @param partitionLeaderEpoch The partition leader epoch\n     * @param records The records to include\n     * @return A new MemoryRecords\n     */\n    public static MemoryRecords withIdempotentRecords(byte This class handles the serialization and\n * deserialization of record batches in the Kafka wire format.\n *\n * <p>\n * The binary schema for a magic v2 record batch is:\n * <pre>\n * RecordBatch =>\n *  BaseOffset => Int64\n *  Length => Int32\n *  PartitionLeaderEpoch => Int32\n *  Magic => Int8\n *  CRC => Uint32\n *  Attributes => Int16\n *  LastOffsetDelta => Int32 // also serves as LastSequenceDelta\n *  BaseTimestamp => Int64\n *  MaxTimestamp => Int64\n *  ProducerId => Int64\n *  ProducerEpoch => Int16\n *  BaseSequence => Int32\n *  RecordsCount => Int32\n *  Records => [Record]\n * </pre>\n * </p>\n *\n * <p>\n * <strong>Thread Safety:</strong> This class is NOT thread-safe. The underlying ByteBuffer may be modified\n * by operations like {@link #setMaxTimestamp(TimestampType, long)}, {@link #setPartitionLeaderEpoch(int)},\n * and {@link #setLastOffset(long)}. Callers must ensure external synchronization if shared across threads.\n * </p>\n *\n * <p>\n * <strong>Key Implementation Details:</strong>\n * <ul>\n *   <li>The CRC covers the data from the attributes to the end of the batch (i.e. all the bytes that follow the CRC).\n *       The partition leader epoch field is not included in the CRC computation.</li>\n *   <li>On Compaction: Unlike older message formats, magic v2 preserves the first and last offset/sequence numbers\n *       from the original batch when the log is cleaned. This is required to restore the producer's state.</li>\n *   <li>Empty batches may be retained to preserve producer sequence information until a new sequence number is written\n *       by the producer or the producer ID expires.</li>\n *   <li>The BaseTimestamp field reflects the timestamp of the first record in the batch in most cases.\n *       If the batch is empty, it is set to -1 (NO_TIMESTAMP).
